Discovery of Large Coal Mine in Heilongjiang Province

Location near Hegang Mine

Estimated Area of Over One Hundred Square Li

Sufficient for Six Hundred Years of Mining

Harbin Dispatch: The Hegang coalfield in Heilongjiang Province has long been known for its richness. However, this was based on geological speculation. The actual discovered coal reserves were only a few square li. After Wan Guobin was appointed by Heilongjiang Province to take over the mine, the good upper coal seams were gradually exhausted. Observers stated that the Hegang coal mine must actively excavate large shafts to extract the lower coal seams. However, the cost of excavating coal shafts requires millions of dollars, which is impossible when the mine lacks capital. Recently, the mine hired geologist Ding Zaijun and mining expert Chen Jiasan to inspect the mine and dispatched personnel to explore and test it. After three months of work near the Hegang coal mine, three coal seams were discovered, forming a large coal mine of over one hundred square li. The total reserves are estimated at 226.55 million tons. If more than one thousand tons are mined daily, it can supply mining for six hundred years. Among them, the portion available for mining in Mingshan has as much as 28.5 million tons. If one thousand tons are extracted daily, it can supply mining for eighty years. Exploration is currently ongoing, and future discoveries are immeasurable. The Heilongjiang Provincial authorities plan to raise a large amount of capital to expand the mining operations at the Hegang coal mine after all exploration is completed. (23rd)

Commencement of Surveying for the Qi-Hei Railway

The Heilongjiang Provincial Government has decided to construct it.

Construction will begin after the spring thaw next year.

Harbin Dispatch: The Qi-Hei Railway, a trunk line traversing over 800 li from Qiqihar to Daheihe in the northeastern half of Heilongjiang Province, was originally proposed in the first year of the Republic of China. At that time, the Russo-Asiatic Bank, entrusted by the Chinese Eastern Railway, requested China to sign an agreement for it to undertake the construction as a Sino-Russian joint venture. Surveyors were dispatched, and line maps were drawn, ready to commence work. However, the European War broke out, followed by the Russian Revolution. Zhu Qinglan, the former General of Heilongjiang, announced the abolition of the original agreement, and China recovered the right to build it independently. Because the line map passed through many mountains, ridges, rivers, and canals, the construction of culverts and bridges would require too much money, causing a delay of more than ten years with no one proposing it. It was not until the era of Chang Yin-huai, who headed Heilongjiang, that the matter was re-deliberated, partly to establish his own power and partly in view of the enthusiastic immigration and increasing number of reclaimers. In recent years, the Heilongjiang Provincial authorities have deeply understood that the construction of railways not only facilitates transportation but also has great benefits for the national economy and people's livelihood. Moreover, the Hu-Hai, Tao-Ang, Qi-Ke and other roads built in recent years have achieved remarkable results, so they decided to build this road. After discussions by the Heilongjiang Provincial Government Committee, a budget was prepared, and a concrete plan was formulated. All matters concerning the proposed construction funding and material procurement have been discussed and resolved. In mid-October of this year, Chief Technician Wu of the Qi-Ke Road and fourteen other scholars were assigned to form a survey team. They departed from the provincial capital towards Heihe in early November. Starting from Moergen, they reached Heihe on November 26. They plan to pass through Qionghui, Qike, and Longzhen, returning to Moergen. The round trip is on two lines, and they will conduct detailed surveys separately to prepare for submission to the provincial government for selection of construction. It is estimated that surveying will be completed in another month, and construction will begin after the thaw next year. This line passes through areas rich in forests and minerals. After the opening of traffic, it will add a major source of wealth to the Northeast. (23rd)

The Farmers' Association Law Passed by the Legislative Yuan (Continued)

Chapter IV: Staff, (Article 19) Each county/city farmers' association subordinate to the provincial farmers' association, and each lower-level farmers' association, shall have one director-general and one deputy director-general, and three to five staff members, who shall be elected by the general membership meeting. (Article 20) The provincial farmers' association shall have five to nine directors, three to five supervisors, three alternate directors, and two alternate supervisors, who shall be elected by the general membership meeting. (Article 21) Farmers' associations above the district level may, with the approval of the competent supervisory authority, establish councillors, who shall be elected by the general membership meeting. (Article 22) Farmers' association staff shall report to the competent supervisory authority and forward to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for record within fifteen days of taking office. (Article 23) The staff elected by the farmers' association shall be honorary positions. (Article 24) If any of the following circumstances apply to a member of staff of the farmers' association, they shall be dismissed immediately: 1. With unavoidable reasons, the general membership meeting resolves to approve their resignation; 2. Neglecting duties, the general membership meeting resolves to order their retirement; 3. In violation of laws and regulations in their duties, engaging in corruption and malfeasance, or engaging in other serious improper conduct, the general membership meeting resolves to order their retirement, or the Ministry of Industry and Commerce or the competent supervisory authority orders their retirement; 4. If any of the circumstances in Article 17 occur.

Chapter V: Meetings (Article 25) Meetings of the farmers' association shall be divided into regular meetings and extraordinary meetings, convened by the director-general or the board of directors. (Article 26) Resolutions of the farmers' association general membership meeting shall be adopted with the attendance of more than half of the members and the consent of more than half of the members present. (Article 27) Resolutions on the following matters shall be adopted with the attendance of more than half of the members and the consent of more than two-thirds of the members present: 1. Amendment of the articles of association; 2. Expulsion of members; 3. Retirement of staff; 4. Election of liquidators and resolutions on matters relating to liquidation. Chapter VI: Expenses (Article 28) Farmers' association expenses shall be divided into two types: 1. Administrative expenses, borne by the members; 2. Project expenses, raised by the farmers' association, but where necessary, may be subsidised by the local administrative authority. (Article 29) In addition to submitting the farmers' association's receipts and expenditures annually to the competent supervisory authority and forwarding to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for record, they shall be notified to all members.

Chapter VII: Supervision (Article 30) The supervisory authorities of farmers' associations shall be as stipulated below: 1. The supervisory authority of the provincial farmers' association shall be the provincial government; 2. The supervisory authorities of county farmers' associations, city farmers' associations, and farmers' associations at all lower levels shall be the county government or the city government.

Chapter VIII: Dissolution and Liquidation (Article 31) The dissolution of a farmers' association shall be as follows: 1. If the resolution of the farmers' association general membership meeting violates the law and the circumstances are serious, the supervisory authority may order its dissolution, but it must be approved by the superior authority or the Ministry of Industry and Commerce; 2. With the attendance of more than two-thirds of the members and the consent of more than two-thirds of the members present, the general membership meeting may resolve to dissolve, but it must be approved by the supervisory authority. (Article 32) When a farmers' association is dissolved under the first clause of the preceding article, its liquidator shall be appointed by the supervisory authority; when dissolved under the second clause of the preceding article, its liquidator shall be elected by the general membership meeting. If an election cannot be held, it shall be appointed by the supervisory authority. (Article 33) The liquidator shall have the power to represent the farmers' association and perform all matters related to liquidation. (Article 34) The method by which the liquidator liquidates and disposes of the property shall be approved by the supervisory authority or resolved by the farmers' association general membership meeting.

Chapter IX: Supplementary Provisions (Article 35) Implementing regulations of this law shall be separately formulated. (Article 36) This law shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Local Dispatches

Qingpu

Two Robbery Cases: The home of Gu Fengchun, a farmer in Du Lai Village, was suddenly attacked by a bandit boat with several bandits on board the other night. They rummaged through boxes and chests, searching and looting at will, but there were no valuables, and only a hundred or so yuan were robbed. In Du Jia Village, sixteen bandits speaking with a northern accent and holding sharp blades suddenly arrived in the middle of the night. They searched the Yin-owned fishing boat first parked in the river, then went to the Chen Xingyu's house, broke down the door and entered, and plundered at will. Because the victim shouted for help, several men and women were wounded by blades. They left at about 3 a.m. the next morning. The total loss was several hundred yuan. The case has been reported to the county government for investigation. New Education Bureau Director Takes Office: Since the former director of the County Education Bureau, Yang Lucun, resigned, the Education Department immediately appointed Yuan Weiwen to take over. However, Yuan has not taken office for four or five months, causing the county's education to be almost at a standstill for half a year. It is understood that Yuan arrived at the bureau the other day, and will take over matters first, and will be sworn in on another date.

Songjiang

Water Police Captain Rescues Hostage: Ding Ziren, the manager of the No. 2 Factory of the Shanghai New Flour Mill, was kidnapped by bandits in front of the factory on the 19th of this month, and a large ransom was demanded, but there has been no news of him. Gong Guozhen of the 3rd Squad of the 1st Water Police Team, after receiving a report from an informant, personally led Inspector Yuan Changbiao to search a firewood boat moored at Zhongdu Bridge. The bandits, seeing the police, immediately went ashore to escape. The water police opened fire to pursue them, killing a young girl on the boat. The bandits all fled. Ding Ziren, who had been held in the boat for several days, was finally rescued.

Sun Xiangyun Kidnapping Case Opens: The case of Sun Xiangyun's kidnapping near Zhu Jia Hang in Xinzhuang has been pending for many months. After repeated investigations by the water and land police, suspects Liu A Si, Yu Fu Gen, Huang Miao Gen, Yang Jin Lin, Lu Jin Sheng, Sun Shou Mei and others were apprehended. The prosecutor's office concluded the investigation and filed a lawsuit in the county court. Judge Huang appointed lawyer Wu Lvping for Liu A Si and Yu Fu Gen for mandatory defense, and Sun Shou Mei also hired Chen Qiushi as his defense. Plaintiff Sun Xu Shi and Sun Bao Yun commissioned lawyer Yuan Xihao to appear in court. At 10 am on the 29th, Judge Li ascended to the criminal court and summoned the suspects for questioning, but the confessions varied. Lawyer Wu raised various points and requested the court to reinvestigate. The plaintiff argued that the defendants had already confessed, requesting sentencing in accordance with the criminal provisions of the indictment. After a lengthy debate, it was heard that the judge had approved a reinvestigation and adjourned the sentencing.

Kunshan

Dashu Town Robbed by Bandits: Dashu Town in Changpu Township of this county is located on the shore of Dianshan Lake and has always been an area where lake bandits appear. At 8 pm on the 26th, two bandit boats arrived, carrying thirty to forty lake bandits ashore. They first cut off the telephone line, then robbed door to door, and dozens of shops in the town were spared. They did not stop until 10 pm, then lined up to get on the boat, and kidnapped two people, heading towards Dianshan Lake. Wei Renzheng, the director of the Zhangpu Public Security Bureau, rushed armed police officers to pursue after receiving the report, but the bandits had already gone far away.

Wuxi

The Story of Han Zhuang's Martyr: Chen Xingxian, a resident living at No. 2, Xinglong Bridge, Beili Chengjiao, Xiyi, has been making a living by running Han Zhuang. The Zhuang flower, named Hua Li Shi, is a 27-year-old from Suzhou, with a cunning face. Young men were enchanted by her charm. Recently, a guest, Du A Er, 29 years old, lived in Qian Cai County and worked as a partner in a tobacco shop. Du saw Hua Li Shi's charming appearance, and a thought of sensual pleasures arose. They hooked up with each other, and gradually became lovers. They stayed in the village for eight nights in a row. Until the night before, Du A Er was exhausted, and his body became as soft as cotton, on the verge of death. Seeing this, Hua Li Shi quickly got up, put on clothes, and reported to the Zhuang owner, asking for help. At dawn, the Zhuang owner Chen Xingxian immediately sent someone to notify Du A Er's family. Du's wife, Zhang, requested Du A Er's friend, Gui Mi A Si, to go to Han Zhuang and carry Du A Er back home. The life was prolonged until yesterday morning, and Du died. Du told his wife before he died that there was a wallet with 107 yuan in it, which was left in Chen Xingxian's home. Seeing that her husband was dead, Du Zhang had to prepare the coffin by herself. She went to Chen Xingxian's home to ask for the relics. Chen Xingxian returned the wallet and flashlight. Du Zhang inspected the wallet, found it empty, and asked Chen Xingxian to hand over the money. Chen Xingxian refused to admit that she had hidden the money, so the two sides quarreled. They reported it to the police. The patrolman took the household Zhu You Shi, Chen Xingxian, Hua Li Shi, and others, to the first branch of the Public Security Bureau. Inspector Qin opened the court and put Song You Shi on trial for allowing prostitution, and sentenced her to 15 days of detention. Chen Xingxian was sentenced to 10 days of detention for being a matchmaker, injuring customs. Hua Li Shi was sentenced to 15 days of detention for adultery with a guest, and her actions were not inspected.

Long-Distance Telephone Calls to Nine Counties on New Year's Day: The long-distance telephones in Wujin and other nine counties have been set up by the Engineering Team of the Electrical Industry Management Office of Jiangsu Province. The telephone poles and wires in Wujin, Yixing and this county have been completely erected. It is scheduled to officially open the calls on New Year's Day next year. First, it can talk to Yixing, and it can also be transferred to Changxing, Hangzhou and other places. As for the Suzhou-Wujiang line, the planting of poles and hanging of wires is in progress, and it will take three weeks to open the call.

Changshu

Police Officer, Doctor, and Editor Conspire to Defraud Money Case: Zhang Guoxian, a native of Dongcang Street outside Xiaodongmen in this county, is eighteen years old and addicted to opium. In early June, someone reported to the Third Police Station of the Public Security Bureau, and Police Officer Xu Jinjian sent police to arrest Zhang and others. Then, Xie Sheng San, the editor of the Ta Kung Pao, interceded and asked Zhang to pay 540 yuan to leave the country, which Zhang agreed to, and wrote a promissory note for 300 yuan as Xie's reward. It is said that Police Officer Xu wanted Zhang to be handed over to the county judiciary due to procedural relationship. Xie Sheng San forged a certificate from Zhang Chongxi, the director of Haiyu Hospital, certifying that Zhang Guoxian had quit smoking in the hospital and had been successfully detoxified, so as to confuse the judge during the trial. Shen Cheng, the trial officer, determined that the director of Haiyu Hospital was not an official doctor, and issued a letter to Jishan Hospital for verification. It was found that Zhang was still addicted to opium, and Zhang was sentenced to two months in prison and a fine of 260 yuan. Xie Sheng San again demanded the money from Zhang based on the promissory note, and Zhao Shaogu (a teacher in the county), Zhang's maternal uncle, discovered that he was defrauding money and sued the county judiciary. Xie Sheng San was arrested first. The county government summoned the plaintiffs and defendants, and Police Officer Xu Jinjian, Doctor Zhang Chongxi, and Police Chief Hu Derong and other ten people for investigation on the afternoon of the 27th. According to the plaintiff Zhang Guoxian, the police came to catch opium at the third police station on the 18th of this month. Xie Sheng San, the editor of the Ta Kung Pao, came to mediate, saying that he knew the county magistrate and the trial officer, so it didn't matter. As long as money was used, Xie Sheng San said that 540 yuan was handed over to Police Officer Xu Jinjian, and he only received two promissory notes for 300 yuan. Police Officer Jin said that he knew nothing. Dr. Zhang Chongxi said that Zhang Guoxian had come to him to quit smoking, and Xie Sheng San introduced him. However, when Zhang Guoxian was questioned, he did not go to quit smoking, and the certificate was obtained by Xie Sheng San. Therefore, the judge determined that the three had conspired to defraud money and arrested Zhang Chongxi, the director of Haiyu Hospital, Xu Jinjian, the police officer of the Third Police Station, and Xie Sheng San, the editor of the Ta Kung Pao. The next day, the General Bureau of Public Security dismissed Hu Derong, the police chief of the Third Police Station, and others.

Changzhou

The Newly Appointed County Magistrate Zhang Arrives in Changzhou: Wu Deyao, the magistrate of Wuyi County, was transferred to Taicang, and Zhang Zhuzhu (courtesy name Yase) , the magistrate of Siyang County, was transferred to Changzhou to take over. County Magistrate Zhang is scheduled to arrive in Changzhou by Jinghu train on the 29th. His younger brother, Yanan, and four or five clerks arrived in Changzhou first on the afternoon of the 28th.

The Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the County Chamber of Commerce: The Wuyi County Chamber of Commerce held a joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees on the afternoon of the 28th, and elected President Yu to preside over the meeting. The resolutions were as follows: (1) In accordance with the resolution of the Wu Wu meeting on December 16, December 31 shall be the deadline for settlement of accounts, and all accounts shall be collected and settled. It shall not be later than February 15 of the 20th year. From the 17th to the 20th, it will be a period of reorganization for shops in various industries. All matters concerning the continuation of shop affairs and the recruitment and dismissal of shop assistants shall be decided during the reorganization period. (2) Send a letter to the Shipping Bureau requesting them to send police teams to prevent navigation in order to maintain the safety of passengers. (3) Notify various industries that the donation for the canal must be submitted to the Association before the collapse to meet emergency needs.

Robbery and Homicide in the Third District: The home of Shi Shuhu, a farmer in Tangjia Village, Nanxing Township, the third district of Wuyi, was suddenly robbed at 11:00 p.m. the other night. Chen, Shuhu's wife, saw that the situation was not good and wanted to go to the attic, but was shot and killed by the bandits with two bullets in a row. The robbers fled north after the incident. The district office reported the case to the county government and the county court on the 28th and requested the arrest.

Jiangyin

Robbery Cases Abound at the End of the Year: The bandit forces in the western countryside are becoming more and more rampant, and robberies and kidnappings occur frequently. On the 26th, the home of Chen Youlin in Daijiadian, Shengang, was robbed and looted, and his six-year-old son was kidnapped and demanded to pay 1,000 yuan in three days. In Hui Di of Chou Zhuangxi, the clan hall of the Min family in Houmei Minjiadai, where the clan chief Min Jinyi received 200 yuan in rent, was robbed by bandits the other night. Chen Qinshu's home in Lanmensha was robbed the other night. His son crossed the river and asked for help from the nearby salt patrol. The bandits heard the gunfire and fled. Sun Cailang's home in Zhangjiagang, the second district, received a threatening letter on the 23rd, requiring a loan of 1,000 yuan to be paid within five days. On the night before last, more than ten bandits broke in and robbed, losing 1,000 yuan. Xue Zijing's home in Daxu, Sansheng Town, was also robbed by bandits the other night, losing more than 1,000 yuan. Before leaving, they demanded 300 yuan to be paid within a week and went to Wushan. Cao Daqiao, a native of Jingjiang, visited his brother in Hengshan Bridge, Wujin yesterday (26th). He encountered a bandit on the way through Yejimiao in Xiagang. He was captured by the local security team. After questioning, it was found that he was a bandit named Tai Rongda, who was wanted by the former county magistrate Ren during his tenure. He was sent to the county yesterday for trial and detention.

Xiaoshan

Military and Police Search Tonghui Gong Yarn Factory: The Xiaoshan County Government Public Security Bureau received a secret report stating that there were many Sheng bandits in the remaining 45 rooms and 43 rooms of the Tonghui Gong Yarn Factory outside Dongmen, and there were many wooden shells. Please order the team to search and arrest them to ensure local security. After receiving the report, Director Gao immediately telegraphed the People's Hall and sent a large platoon of security teams, and telegraphed the Ren County Public Security Bureau to send a platoon of security teams, and four patrol police teams and four police teams of the bureau. Director Gao and Team Leader Zheng, Inspector Chen and Police Officer Chen led the team to rush to the area on the evening of the 25th to search house by house. It is a pity that the bandits had already fled upon hearing the news, so nothing was found.

Request to Rebuild the Dangerous Xiao-Shao Causeway: The Xiao-Shao Causeway has always been built by raising funds locally. Later, due to the danger of the causeway project and the lack of funds, the causeway lottery was issued. It was merged into the Qiantang River Engineering Bureau in the sixteenth year, and then merged into the Water Conservancy Bureau last year. Due to limited funding, repairs were neglected. Engineer Dong of Shao-Xiao Gate has reported that the causeway body of 314 and a half zhang from Sunjia Ferry to Lao Shi Causeway has many cracks and is very dangerous. He has formulated a repair plan and approved a budget of more than 85,000 yuan for the causeway project. He requested the Department of Construction to forward it to the provincial government for approval, so as to raise funds and start construction.

Nantong

Coastal Bandit Prevention Facilities: Recently, the coastal area of Nantong and Haimen counties has been unsettled. Therefore, coastal defense was jointly arranged. Blockhouses were built at the mouths of Sanyu Lusi, a special patrol team was formed, and the water patrol team patrolled various ports. During the winter defense period, military telephones were temporarily installed along the coast.

The Provincial Security Corps Xu Ying Concentrates in Tongcheng: The Provincial Security Corps Xu Ying was ordered to leave Sanyang Town for Liyang, and concentrated in Tongcheng. After the National Army Liang Guanying's troops come to Tong for takeover, they will leave Tong.

Jiangbei Counties Implement Pacification: Jiangsu Province launched pacification, first implemented in Jiangbei. At this moment, the police teams and civil corps of various counties are under the command and dispatch of Director Zhang.

Pinghu

Xu Wenfu Escapes from Bandits: Xu Wenfu, who was abducted in the robbery case in Xian Da Village, is the head of the village's security team and village chief. He usually has a self-important behavior, so he has many complaints. Since being kidnapped, his family has entrusted people to inquire everywhere, but there has been no news. Now the bandits have found that Xu is not wealthy, but just a small well-off family, and have voluntarily lowered the price for his release. He has escaped from the bandits the other day and released to return home.

Zhang Yan's Regular Ship Robbed: Zhang Yan's regular ship left the town yesterday. When passing through Xinmiao Town in the eastern territory of Yaqian, it was suddenly encountered by bandits who boarded the ship and searched, taking away 4,000 to 5,000 yuan in cash that the town's shops had sent to the money shop in the city.

Anecdotes of Robbing Xinpu Town: One or two days before the town was robbed, many people disguised as hawkers, selling spiced dried tofu, or pickled mustard greens, dried radishes, etc., and broke into wealthy homes everywhere, claiming to be selling, secretly surveying the route, and staying overnight in the hotel opened by Jia Lao Si at night. Therefore, this time, the Bei Shi and Zhong Shi were robbed house by house, and none were spared. The Nan Bei Pawnshops, Changhao Rice Shop, Soybean Cake Shop, and Tianlun Cloth Shop were all robbed, only Nanshi suffered less damage because more than a dozen anti-smuggling patrol boats were moored, firing shots to show their power, such as Taiji Wood Shop and others did not suffer.

Huzhou

Hostage Peng Zhengfa Shot to Death: Peng Zhengfa, a resident of Fangjia Yang near Shizuka, a village in the southern district of Huzhou, was robbed by bandits and abducted last month. It is heard that Peng's family has entrusted people to negotiate everywhere, but it has been a long time and there has been no clue. A few days ago, Peng's family suddenly received a letter from a villager in Changshu, saying that a hostage named Peng Zhengfa who had been kidnapped by bandits had been shot to death on the way. Peng's wife immediately asked her relative Yu to go to Changshu to inquire. According to the villagers, a group of bandits were attacked by the police a few days ago, and each bandit fled elsewhere. The hostage Peng Zhengfa was accidentally hit by a bullet and was seriously injured. The bandits abandoned Peng here. After Peng was shot, he could still speak, and told the circumstances of the kidnapping and the address of his hometown, and asked to send a letter to notify his family to come and claim him. He died at dusk. According to Yu, after returning to the village and contacting Peng's wife, he prepared the necessary items and went to Changshu to collect the coffin and return home on the other day.

The Head of the Changxing Detective Team is Suspected of Colluding with Bandits: Since Team Leader Wang Ziqi took over the Second Security Team of this city, he has spared no effort in suppressing bandits. It is heard that Team Leader Wang went to the western village for inspection a few days ago. When he went to a place belonging to Changxing County, he heard that Wang Jinrong, the head of the Detective Team of the County Public Security Bureau, and Xu Junyou, the detective, and Song Waizui and Xiao Pangzi, the detectives, were suspected of colluding with bandits. Therefore, yesterday he personally escorted the gang to Huzhou and planned to investigate in detail before handling the case.

Important News

The Protracted Tsinghua University President Issue

Students Request Chairman Chiang to Appoint a President Quickly

| Nominating Zhou Yichun, Zhao Yuanren, and Hu Shih |

Since the issue of the Tsinghua University president arose, it has been over half a year. Although the students have expressed their opinions on the selection of a successor, the true state of affairs internally and the reasons why the Ministry of Education has not yet made a statement remain largely unknown to the outside world. Some speculate that Tsinghua's abundant funding and beautiful environment have attracted many aspirants, which, although conjecture, is not entirely without basis. We have obtained a collection of telegrams and documents sent by the university's student union to the Ministry of Education this semester, disclosed as follows: Telegram of October 19th, "To Minister Chiang of the Ministry of Education in Nanjing: Our university's students firmly oppose Luo Jialun's return to the university. Please approve his resignation quickly. Tsinghua University Student Union, Hao." Telegram of November 15th, "To Minister Chiang of the Ministry of Education in Nanjing: The entire student body has resolved in a general assembly to request that you promptly approve Luo Jialun's resignation and appoint one of the three gentlemen, Zhou Yichun, Zhao Yuanren, or Hu Shih, as his successor. Tsinghua University Student Union, Xian." Letter of November 18th, "Regarding the request for the prompt approval of Luo Jialun's resignation and the selection of a worthy successor to maintain the university's operations and benefit education: The issue of our university's president has been in dispute for a long time. Since the departure of former President Luo Jialun, the university's affairs have been left in a state of uncertainty for several months. The students earnestly hope that you will have a fair solution. We have repeatedly telegraphed our request for the early approval of Mr. Luo's resignation, hoping to gain your understanding. However, a few months ago, we read your telegram to the university's council, which did not heed the students' public request but insisted on retaining Mr. Luo and temporarily assigning someone as an agent. We were greatly shocked. An investigation revealed that Mr. Luo's departure was partly due to the reasonable demands of the entire student body and partly due to his own recognition of the difficulties and withdrawal. With feelings as opposed as ice and charcoal, there is no possibility of his return. The country is full of capable individuals, and there is theoretically no need for his return. The students only hope that the successor will be a capable person who can ensure that they can study in peace. Why would you insist on retaining Mr. Luo, creating more disputes? The students know that the authority to decide on the president's appointment and removal rests with you, but the key to education lies in finding the right person. The president is the master of a university and is related to the future of the nation. His knowledge and character should be admired by the students internally and praised by society externally, so that he can lead with a gentle breeze and nurture future generations. Mr. Luo served as president of our university for two years, but there was no actual progress in the university's affairs, and incidents regarding his departure have occurred several times. This shows that he is not suitable for our university. If there is disagreement, he should leave. Mr. Luo himself has seen this, but you insist on retaining him, which we, the students, cannot understand after much contemplation. Holding our books, we are deeply worried and restless. Therefore, on November 5th, the entire student body unanimously passed a resolution to request again that you promptly approve Mr. Luo's resignation and appoint one of the three gentlemen, Zhou Yichun, Zhao Yuanren, or Hu Shih, as his successor. These three gentlemen are fully qualified to shoulder heavy responsibilities and have a character that can win people's respect. Their knowledge and experience are in line with the high expectations. We believe you are already familiar with them. We have already telegraphed everything on the 15th and reiterate our previous request, sincerely asking you to appoint talented people for the sake of the country and grant our request to maintain the university's operations and benefit education. All matters concerning the request for the prompt approval of Luo Jialun's resignation as president of our university and the selection of one of the three gentlemen, Zhou Yichun, Zhao Yuanren, or Hu Shih, as his successor, are respectfully submitted in writing for your consideration. We would be eternally grateful. Respectfully presented to Minister Chiang of the Ministry of Education." Letter of December 24th to Chairman Chiang, "Regarding the request for the swift appointment of a president to benefit the university's operations: Unfortunately, the issue of the president of our university has been ongoing for over half a year. Although the university council has maintained operations and prevented the interruption of studies, a group without a leader will inevitably stir up trouble. A university without a president may lead to malicious schemes. We have previously telegraphed the Ministry of Education repeatedly, requesting a swift resolution, hoping to gain your understanding. Our university's opposition to Luo Jialun is purely out of sincere love for the university and is the unanimous demand of the entire student body. Judging from the resolutions of the student body's general assemblies, almost no one sympathizes with Mr. Luo. The situation can be easily imagined. Furthermore, what is Mr. Luo's character, knowledge, qualifications, and abilities? You have surely seen everything clearly and know it well. We fear that rumors from afar may be inaccurate and that malicious individuals may exaggerate, attempting to unjustly tarnish our university's reputation. Therefore, we must present the facts again. Now, the selection of presidents for various national universities has been announced and they have assumed their positions. Only our Tsinghua University has not yet found a suitable solution. Although this is due to the Ministry's cautious selection, we fear that unforeseen events may occur, making it difficult to deal with. Good intentions may lead to bad results, which is not your original intention in promoting education. Regarding the selection of a president, the student body's general assembly previously unanimously passed the following conditions: (1) Rich in educational experience, (2) Profound knowledge, (3) Well-established reputation, (4) Noble character, (5) Non-partisan, (6) Truly capable of developing Tsinghua. Based on these conditions, we recommend selecting one of the three gentlemen, Zhou Yichun, Zhao Yuanren, or Hu Shih. We have always believed that you are enthusiastic about education and concerned about the future of our university. Therefore, we dare to express our opinions and sincerely request that you grant our request and appoint a president as soon as possible. It would be fortunate for the party and the country, and fortunate for our university. As for the details, we believe Mr. Qian Changzhao has already conveyed them. All matters concerning the request for the swift selection and appointment of a suitable president to benefit the university's operations are respectfully submitted in writing for your consideration. We await your instructions. Respectfully presented to Chiang, Chairman of the National Government and concurrently in charge of the Ministry of Education."

The Director of the Zhejiang Education Department Took Office Yesterday

Chen Bulei sent a telegram from Nanjing to the Zhejiang Education Department on the 27th, stating that the newly appointed Director, Zhang Daofan, would arrive in Zhejiang on the 28th. He himself was unable to come to Zhejiang due to his busy ministerial duties, so he specially dispatched former Secretary Lin Duanfu to the department to handle the handover. After receiving the telegram, the Education Department, although previously observing Japanese holidays, remained open as usual to handle the handover matters. Director Zhang Daofan arrived in Hangzhou around 1:00 PM on the 28th and stayed at the West Lake Hotel. He then met with Chairman Zhang at the residence to discuss everything and went to the department on the morning of the 29th to inspect. The official swearing-in ceremony will be held after the central government appoints a supervisor.

The Municipal Education Bureau Orders Municipal Schools and Institutions to Observe the National Calendar New Year Holiday

The Municipal Education Bureau yesterday issued an order to its affiliated schools and institutions, stating: "According to the Municipal Government's Order No. 6847, which states that, according to the Executive Yuan's telegram, the central government has now revised the National Calendar New Year holiday to five days, from December 31st to January 4th. All sectors must not close for the Lunar New Year in order to promote the National Calendar and change people's customs. In addition to complying with the order, it is hereby telegraphed in advance, hoping that you will instruct your subordinates to comply accordingly." Upon receiving this, in addition to issuing separate orders, we hereby order the schools and affiliated institutions in this city to comply accordingly.

Peng Xiang Resigns from Labour University

Since the new president of Labour University of this city was announced and someone is in charge, all staff and students of the university are grateful to former President Yi and have high hopes for the future of the university. Peng Xiang, the former chairman of the university council, secretary-general, and acting dean of the School of Social Sciences, announced his resignation and departure from the university yesterday due to exhaustion from his efforts in university affairs over the past two years. He also issued a notice to all faculty and students, stating that he had limited knowledge and felt ashamed for not accomplishing anything during his year at the university. He originally intended to retire during the summer vacation to avoid blame, but the university faced many difficulties and the president resigned. Seeing that the arduous efforts of the past three years were about to be destroyed, he had to temporarily maintain the university's operations. Fortunately, the university's foundation has been stabilized, and the new president has arrived and taken office. The rumors of "takeover," "shutdown," and "no president appointed" have not materialized. Therefore, the purpose of his previous tolerance and remaining at the university has been fully achieved, and it is time for him to fulfill his original intention, resign from his position, and leave the university. In addition to handing over university affairs to the new president, this announcement is hereby made. Peng Xiang, December 29, 1920.

Liao Maoru's Statement Regarding the Guanghua University Incident

Liao Maoru's statement regarding the Guanghua University incident is as follows:

Many discussions and declarations from various parties regarding the recent Guanghua University incident have involved me. My ambition has always been to study education. For the past ten years, I have never been involved in political issues other than education, nor have I published any articles. My friends and teachers know this well, so there is no need for me to argue. Even in terms of my dedication to education, I prefer teaching to administration. However, I have often been forced to do things against my will due to circumstances. I recall that when I first joined Guanghua in 1927, I reluctantly took the position of director of the affiliated high school. A year later, President Zhang Yongniang forced me to concurrently serve as vice president, and I repeatedly refused. Subsequently, I repeatedly requested to resign, but the president firmly retained me. During that time, I received invitations from Tsinghua University in Beiping, Zhongshan University in Guangdong, Central University in Nanjing, and the China-America Educational and Cultural Foundation, but I did not accept any of them. Last year, the position of director of the Chinese Education Department of the工部局 was already agreed upon, but it was stopped due to the president's insistence on retaining me. The following is a copy of my resignation letter from last semester:

"To President: I love Guanghua, and I also love myself. For the past three years, I have been working for Guanghua without considering everything. However, my health is weak. I have not left administrative life for a single day in the past ten years since returning to China. Recently, I have been taking care of both the university and middle school departments, and I feel even more exhausted and irritable. After participating in the National Education Conference in the spring, I suffered from coughing. At that time, I planned to ask the president to relieve me of some administrative duties, but the school was preparing for the fifth anniversary, so I did not want to speak up. Now that the academic year is coming to an end, the university and middle school departments have taken shape, and development is not difficult. However, my spirit has become increasingly exhausted. If I continue to force myself to support, it will not only not help the school, but also harm myself. Therefore, I sincerely request that the president approve my request for a one-year leave to rest at home or allow me to teach a few hours at Guanghua until my strength recovers, and then I will repay the school. During this semester, I have declined all invitations from various parties (Chen Bulei, director of Zhejiang Province, Central University, and Wuxi Public Education College have all sent letters). I have refused them all because I cannot betray Guanghua." June 8th

The president replied, "I received your letter from Jiading and learned everything. Guanghua's success today is all thanks to you. I value your friendship and believe you are the most sincere. Considering our daily interactions, I cannot bear to be indifferent. From now on, I will be responsible for all financial responsibilities and major difficulties, while the school's management and academic affairs will still rely on you. I sincerely hope that you will not give up. I will say more in person." June 11th

After receiving the letter, I thought that all private universities in Shanghai that have been registered are operating diligently and engaged in construction. Guanghua has a five-year history and a considerable reputation, so I should try to follow suit. Therefore, I overestimated myself and thought of staying for another year or two to work for Guanghua. I became more motivated and did not avoid hard work. After the incident, because it involved me, I decided to listen to the president's solution and left the school immediately. On the 13th, I formally resigned from the school. Regarding the list of expelled students published in the newspaper on the 16th, it was decided by a "six-person committee" organized by the president, and I did not participate in it at all. On the 15th, I received a reply from the president as follows:

"I received your letter and understood everything. The current dispute in the school is nothing more than a temporary emotional impulse of a few students, involving reports of facts. How can we not uphold justice and slander others? You have been working hard and bearing grievances for three years, and everyone knows this. You have repeatedly requested to resign, but I have firmly retained you. This is not the time to protect yourself. Please continue to serve in both the university and middle school departments. In addition to reporting the retention situation to the board of directors, I sincerely ask you to understand everything."

On the 16th, the school sent a letter of retention from the board of directors and a resolution of the board of directors as follows:

"Resolution of the Board of Directors of Guanghua University, 1:00 PM, December 16, 1920, at 10 Moore Road. Directors present: Wang Shengsan, Xu Xinliu, Yu Rizhang, Zhao Jinqing, Zhu Yinjiang, Yu Qiaqing, Wu Yunzhai, Shi Shengzhi, Lin (representing Lin Kanghou), Xin Zhi, Zhang Yongniang. Chairman: Zhang Yongniang. Recorder: Wang Yi. Report Matters: (1) The president reported on the recent dispute involving a few students. (2) The president reported on Vice President Liao's resignation letter and the retention situation. Resolution Matters: (1) Unanimously retained Vice President Liao and encouraged him to overcome difficulties. (2) All other matters concerning the aftermath of the school will be resolved by President Zhang."

On the 17th, I firmly resigned from the school again. This is the entire process of my involvement with Guanghua from beginning to end. All departments of the university and middle school have hired certified Kuomintang instructors. "The memorial week does not adhere to the prescribed time. The school motto can be improved. It was stipulated when Guanghua was first established that if it needs to be changed, it must be proposed by the president. In short, my personal departure is not a problem, and my reputation is not important. But right and wrong must be clear, and justice must be preserved. Therefore, I have briefly recounted the facts for the gentlemen of the country."

The Dunhua Elementary School Founded by the Islamic School Has Been Completed

Construction and Land Purchase Cost Over 100,000 Yuan

Stipulating that Free Students Account for Half of the Enrollment

The China Islamic Association purchased a plot of land on Qinglian Street and built the Dunhua Elementary School. After more than half a year of operation, the school building has now been completed. Classes will begin in early February next year, starting with the first four grades and gradually expanding to accommodate five or six hundred students. The cost of land, construction, and operation totals over 100,000 yuan, which was raised by the Islamic community itself. The school's annual expenses have a fixed income of approximately 4,000 yuan. The school pays attention to the education of poor children, so it stipulates that free students account for half of the enrollment. Although the school is run by Islamic individuals, students are not limited to Muslims and there are no religious courses, which is the same as ordinary elementary schools. The founders are well-known Islamic figures Ma Fuxiang, Ma Linyi, Ha Shaofu, Sha Shanyu, and others.

Pre-Announcement of the Chinese Art Exhibition

The Chinese Art College holds an exhibition of achievements every semester. This semester, a large-scale exhibition will be held. In addition to holding it in Shanghai, it will also be held along the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway, such as in Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Yangzhou, and Nanjing. It is scheduled to open for two days on January 9th and 10th at the Ningbo Native Place Association. This exhibition will feature 300 works of calligraphy and painting from over 90 famous artists outside the school, and 300 works from teachers and students within the school, all of which are the most exquisite selections. In addition, Zhang Hongwei Lay Buddhist's most proud work in his life is the Hundred Flowers Scroll, which has been inscribed by famous artists at home and abroad. It is priced at 3,000 yuan, and all the proceeds from the sale will be donated to the school's expenses. It can be said to be the grandest of exhibitions. These calligraphy and paintings are numbered separately, and each ticket costs 14 yuan. It is said that the purchase of tickets has been extremely enthusiastic in recent days.

Regulations of the Shanghai No. 1 Industrial and Commercial Football Association

The Shanghai No. 1 Public Stadium is organizing the Third Industrial and Commercial Amateur Football Tournament, which was previously reported. It is now known that the regulations have been printed, and many amateur teams have come to inquire about them. It is expected that the number of participating teams in this tournament will be more than the previous one. The regulations are attached below:

(1) The purpose of this association is to promote amateur sports in the industrial and commercial sectors, exercise the body, and improve football skills.

(2) This association has a committee of five members who are responsible for all association affairs and review the qualifications of teams and players.

(3) All amateur football teams in the industrial and commercial sectors, except those with outstanding reputations, may join this association.

(4) All amateur football teams that join this association must not include school students (except for those attending tutoring night classes) or physical education teachers.

(5) Each team is limited to 16 players, and each person is only allowed to join one team. Registration procedures are detailed in the registration form.

(6) Once a team is registered, it may not change players or increase or decrease the number of people. Players who are not registered or whose registration procedures are not complete may not participate in the competition.

(7) Registration dates are from January 4th to January 25th.

(8) The competition rules will be implemented in accordance with the latest Far Eastern Games rules. However, the duration of each game is set at 35 minutes, with a 5-minute break in the middle. If there are fewer than eight players on the field each time, it will be considered a forfeit.

(9) The competition method adopts a single round-robin system (if there are many participating teams, a group single round-robin competition will be used). The winner gets two points, the tie gets one point, and the loser gets zero points. If the scores of two teams are equal, a tiebreaker will be held. If the scores of three or more teams are equal, an elimination competition will be used to determine the champion.

(10) The competition venue is at the Shanghai No. 1 Public Stadium. The competition ball is provided by the association. The referees for the competition are hired by the association.

(11) The competition dates are set for Sunday and Saturday afternoons. Each team must arrive at the venue on time in the order arranged by the association and must not be late. If the weather is rainy and the competition is postponed, you can call Mr. Zhang Longhai at 75 Nanshi for inquiries. If a team has a special event and the game needs to be rescheduled, it must first obtain the consent of the opposing team and jointly submit a letter to the association stating the reasons two days before the game. It will only be valid after being approved by the association.

(12) If a team does not arrive at the venue for the competition without a reason or is 10 minutes late, it will be considered a forfeit. If a team forfeits twice, its competition qualification will be canceled. Once the competition qualification is canceled, all previous competitions will also be canceled and invalid.

(13) If a team or player is accused of violating the rules and regulations, the association will investigate and verify the facts. In minor cases, regardless of the result of the game, it will be considered a failure. In severe cases, the team will never be allowed to participate in the competition.

(14) If a player is penalized by the referee and leaves the field due to a foul during the competition, the vacancy may not be filled.

(15) The team may not protest on the spot during the competition or stop the game on any pretext. A written protest should be submitted to the association committee for resolution within two days after the event. However, the committee's decision is the final judgment, and the protesting team may not object again.

(16) These regulations are valid from the date of commencement of registration to the date of termination. If there are any omissions, the committee may propose amendments.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter Hai Ke

Plaintiff (to his lawyer): Thank you. You have handled my case well.

Lawyer: Yes. Please give me the legal fees as soon as possible to settle the matter.

Plaintiff: About how much will it cost in total?

Lawyer: Including conversation fees, correspondence fees, court appearance fees, etc., all included, it will be about one thousand taels. Your father and I are old friends, so I won’t overcharge you.

Plaintiff: Alas, that is my misfortune. Why weren't you old friends with my ancestors as well?

Old Pastor (asking a drunkard holding a bottle of brandy): Are you planning to finish this bottle of wine by yourself?

Drunkard: No. This bottle of wine was bought jointly with my friend. We each drink half.

Old Pastor: Drinking alcohol is very harmful. It is best for young people not to drink. Can you show that you have the courage to reform and pour your half of the bottle into the gutter by the side of the street?

Drunkard: That won't work. Because my half is in the bottom half of the bottle.

Carpenter: (Working on repairs on the roof of the asylum): Alright, alright. It's almost done.

Madman (sneaking out of his room and climbing onto the roof, suddenly grabbing the carpenter's collar): Hehe. Let's jump down to the street together, shall we?

Carpenter (terrified): Everyone can jump. That's nothing special. How about we go down to the street and jump up to the roof together?

Words of Wisdom from Ma Junwu Wan Cheng

Dr. Ma Junwu, a renowned scholar with a doctorate in engineering from Germany, gave a speech on "The Spirit of Academic Research in Japan" at the Da Xia University Commemoration Week in late May. Having recently returned from his travels in Japan, Dr. Ma felt deeply and his words of wisdom should be recorded. (Excerpts below)

The Japanese use the newest methods of production and the oldest methods of consumption, while the Chinese use the old methods of production from the 16th century and the new methods of consumption from the 20th century. How can the people not be poor and the nation not be weak? The only way out is for the nation to strive to expand and reward investment in academic research. At the same time, it is hoped that the Chinese people will go to libraries and laboratories.

Chinese education is a diploma exchange. Ask students why they want diplomas, and they answer to eat and get a wife. Japanese students often stay in school after graduating from university to continue their studies, demonstrating a true spirit of learning. Dr. Ma Junwu will earnestly teach Chinese students this point and help save China's commercialized education.

Chinese students consider wearing Western suits and leather shoes fashionable, while Japanese students consider being simple and clean an honor. It was once said that a Chinese student studying at Tokyo Imperial University reeked of perfume one day, making people feel drunk. When he entered the laboratory, he was driven out by a Japanese student, who said, "You are like a vagabond, unworthy of academic research." This became a laughing stock for a time. This is also a wake-up call for young people. Japanese students study diligently, often forgetting to eat and drink. Chinese students should take this as a model.

An Evening Chat About Oil-Based Photography Jian Quan

I have always liked photography, but I only know a little about it and have no opportunity to study it in depth. At the current fourth Hua She Exhibition, I saw several oil-based photographs. I felt that their light and color were very different from the ordinary and could not be described by ink and paper. I was eager to dispel my doubts. I used to live in Peiping and often saw large-scale Chinese paintings of landscapes and animals by Mr. Hu Boxiang. His brushwork was superb, powerful and extraordinary, far beyond what contemporary artists could achieve. Recently, I came to Shanghai, and through the introduction of a friend, I had a chance to meet Mr. Hu. So I went to visit him and was received. At that time, Mr. Hu was working on a painting of a fierce tiger under the lamp, and Mr. Zhu Shuren was also present. I was overjoyed because both of them had oil-based photographs on display in this exhibition. I was given a detailed explanation and recorded it as follows for the benefit of fellow enthusiasts. (What the two gentlemen said below.) The term "oil-based" is not very appropriate. It should be called the Mo paper oil color method. Any ordinary enlarged photograph can be used for this. First, put it in bleaching solution to bleach the image, then fix it and dry it. Then you can apply the oil application procedure. Before applying the oil, soak it in clean water at a temperature of about 70 degrees Fahrenheit. The length of soaking time depends on the softness and hardness of the gelatin on the surface of the enlargement paper. After removing it from the water, lay it flat on damp blotting paper and use a clean, damp handkerchief to absorb the moisture from the surface of the paper. Then you can use a special brush to dip the oil color on the tip of the brush and apply it. If you need to reduce the oil color, you can use another brush and lightly tap it to remove it. This kind of surgery is something that anyone can do well as long as they are brave enough to try. The most valuable point is that you can add or delete things from the scenery. However, the danger is also here. If the author lacks aesthetic sense, the result will be a hundred mistakes, and it is better to enlarge directly. Photography is like writing and painting. It is not a masterpiece just because you use famous paper and famous pens. Therefore, the most important foundation of photography is still to promote aesthetics and express individuality. Its structure, color, etc. are also important points. If you focus on a part of the procedure or think about the materials, even if you reach the peak, you are only an ordinary technician in the photography industry. Today, photographic art is very popular internationally. In exhibitions in various countries, many famous works are made using the oil application method. It is even more popular in France and Italy. According to what we know, there are Zhang Zhenhou, Wang Shilian, Lang Jingshan, Gao Mei, Shen Gao, Wang Dafo, Guo Xilin, Xu Junshan, and my younger brother Bozhou who have a deep understanding of this art. This is a clear sign that interest in the domestic photography community is growing.

Miscellaneous Notes from Sichuan Hu Tiannong, Sent from Sichuan

After the death of Tan Yankai, the military and political circles in Sichuan all mourned him passionately. Wu Peifu, who had been hiding in Sichuan for a long time, also wrote a couplet and sent it to the central government. The upper part was inscribed "Brother Zu'an, may you rest in peace." The lower part was boldly inscribed "Your brother, Wu Peifu." The couplet reads: "The road to Shu is difficult, the apes in the Wu Gorge cry tears. In Changsha, I mourn bitterly, the wild geese returning to Hengyang bring several letters." The feelings are evident in the words. Wu is probably the saddest person today.

Also, General Yang Sen, stationed in Qu County, is also extremely passive. He occasionally composes poems, which are quite sad. The poem reads: "The wind and rain hasten the early autumn, the military uniform reminds me of the passing years. My army is poor to the bone, staying here for a long time, I am afraid I will make a home. Thinking of flying geese, I wave my pen like an old crow. Occasionally, I stand upstairs and watch the slanting smoke."

A Record of the Plum Blossom Song and Dance Troupe Zheng

The Plum Blossom Girls' Song and Dance Troupe, led by troupe leader Wei Yingbo, went to various ports on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River to try out new sounds. Wherever they went, their reputation was unprecedented. Recently, they performed at the Municipal Hall on Nanjing Road, and the performances were very popular. Yesterday, I had a little free time and was able to feast my eyes. I will record a few things for the readers.

Flexible like boneless. The excellent dance "The Dying Swan" is extremely difficult to express. Ms. Zhang Qi of the troupe is the best at it. The most commendable thing is that she is graceful and agile. She can raise one foot to her head, and she can also bend her head back to the ground. All of these have reached the realm of perfection.

Flower troupe clusters. This dance involves 12 participants and is purely Western in style. It is directed by Mr. Klarin, a Westerner. Every move is extremely beautiful. Among them, Qian and Zhong Xiu are the most distinctive. Their dance posture is the most unique. Commentators say that the Flower Troupe Clusters dance is the greatest success of the troupe.

"Long Remember" is a song that contains a sense of sadness. The song is not difficult, but it is not easy to convey emotions. Minghui's reputation in the past was based on this. On this day, Zhang Xianlin sang the song clearly, without dance, which added to the quietness. Her voice was as exciting as a warrior going to war, thunderous, and as sad as a cuckoo crying in the middle of the night, deeply touching people. She is indeed a talented woman.

Little Painter. Little Painter is a famous play in the dance world recently. In this troupe, Gong Qiuxia plays the painter, and her performance of the innocent state is perfect. Cai Wenjin and Yang Zhenbiao, the teachers, are especially funny. The applause never stopped at the end.

Celebrate the New Year. This performance at the City Hall has been going on for ten days. It is said that 7,000 to 8,000 yuan have been sold from the 20th to the 27th. The attendance is not weak. The meeting was originally scheduled to end on the 29th. On the 24th, the important officials decided to continue the performance for five days, until the 3rd of the 20th year. A temporary program was arranged. From the 29th to the end of the year, they will perform "Moonlit Night", "Spring Happiness" and ten new songs and dances. From New Year's Day to the 3rd, at the request of all walks of life, they will re-perform "Seven Emotions". The Wuhu Star Theater also hired the Plum Blossom Troupe to perform on stage from New Year's Day. They had no choice but to draw members who had recently been recruited into the troupe with a little foundation in singing and dancing, supplemented by a few old troupe members, to fulfill the contract with Wuhu. Therefore, the performances were limited to plays such as "Little Three Butterflies". In Shanghai, "Seven Emotions", "Li Yantao" and other large song and dance dramas are still being performed. It is said that the Republican Theater will also be performing "Seven Emotions" and other programs on the stage of the Plum Troupe from the 10th to meet the requests of those in Nanshi who love to watch singing and dancing. The magic power of "Seven Emotions" is so great. I know that Ms. Yingbo and Mr. Cai Wenjin, the authors of the play, must be very happy about this.

Short message. Guo Xiaoping, Li Daoxi, and Ni Qiuping are all famous erhu players in Shanghai. Their achievements are vast and broad, and they are known as the Four King Kongs of the time. Recently, the three gentlemen established the China National Phonetic Society and specially hired experts from Peiping to manufacture famous musical instruments for the benefit of fellow enthusiasts. Mr. Li is especially meticulous in the selection of piano materials and the method of matching them. It is as if Yang Baozhong is in the middle of the peace. It is now heard that the opening is scheduled for early next month. Those who want exquisite musical instruments should pay attention. The address of the society is located in the center of the racecourse on Fourth Road in the British Concession, downstairs in the vegetable society. (Piano fans)

Warmth in My Heart (346) Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Sixteen: Cui Xiu Visits Mr. with Diligence to Ask for Words, Qinglou Banquets Female Heroes with Generous Talk of Soldiers

Who knew that after the person who invited the guests returned, he shouted downstairs, "The guest is coming." Since he said that the guest was coming, she would naturally come. All the guests sat upright, waiting for the arrival of this Chinese-German female hero. In less than fifteen minutes, there was a sound of leather shoes on the stairs, and a person walked up and asked where Luyi's room was. The people in the room quickly shouted, "Here, here." The guest strode in, but she was wearing a sapphire blue iron-patterned men's robe. Although the cheongsam worn by women has gradually become popular now, that kind of cheongsam does not have slits at the bottom. There are also fashionable people who make the cheongsam very short, only three or four inches past the knee. However, many people oppose wearing cheongsams because the Xinhai Revolution opposed and overthrew the Manchu Qing government. It has a bit of racial revolution. The Han people were uneasy and depressed for a long time because foreigners entered the Central Plains. This time, they wanted to vent their anger. Therefore, they wanted to overthrow the Manchu system. But isn't the cheongsam worn by women still a Manchu system? Then why should our dignified Han people learn from it? So at that time, wearing cheongsams was not yet popular. Women all wore short skirts. However, like Ren Peizhen today, she refused to claim to be an ordinary woman. She wanted to be like a man. She also wore a man's robe, but she didn't add a jacket or anything like that on the outside. At this time, it was also very fashionable for women to wear men's clothes. Just like Luyi, she often wore men's clothes. Her body was originally petite, and she wore a men's robe. She also wore a vest on the outside, with inlaid ruyi heads around it. She wore a Western-style casual hat on her head, which was also very charming. Not only Luyi, but also many hall waiters were dressed like this.

However, although Ren Peizhen wore a man's robe, she did not wear that kind of Western-style hat. She still had a bun. Looking at her bun, it was indeed a bit unique. It turned out that during the Xinhai Revolution, some aspiring women also had some revolutionary spirit. That revolutionary spirit started with the bun. The bun was combed on the head and neck. In the Qing Dynasty, the buns of women were indeed a bit unsightly. There was a kind of bun combed on the neck. They thought it was charming, like the so-called falling horse bun in ancient times. Some people said that kind of bun was a bit demonic. There was also the kind called the cool bun. The idea was to be simple, but if you were not careful, your hair would fall down. In that year of the revolution, women became popular with a forward bun. They combed their hair on the corners of their foreheads. Some also combed their hair on the top of their heads. At that time, some people also called it the fighting bun, which meant that no matter how much you fought with others, your hair would not fall down.

Travel Notes from Nanyang (116) Hua

People in India and Burma eat a lot of sour and spicy foods, such as onions and garlic, and betel nuts are especially popular.

Most of the livelihoods of the Burmese people depend on the export of rice, but now the British limit exports, saying that they want to maintain the livelihoods of the poor. The Chinese people say, "No, this is cutting off the financial resources of the Burmese people, fearing that their wealth will be active and unfavorable to the British." If rice exports are cut off, all financial resources will be stagnant and undeveloped, which is also one of the reasons for the decline of commerce. Also, because gold is expensive and the cost is high, the export price of rice is high and difficult to sell. The locals suffer losses as a result. Many Chinese people in Burma run machine rice mills, called rice grinders. Their capital ranges from hundreds of thousands to millions.

The climates of the various islands in Nanyang are different due to the different locations. They do not know each other. Taking Burma as an example, there are three seasons. According to the ancient calendar, from April to September is the rainy season, which is very suitable for hygiene. From October to December is the winter season, which is rainless and warm, with a slight chill, making it the most suitable time for work. All industries and commerce are booming at this time. From January to March, it is extremely hot and rainless, making it the least suitable season. The three seasons in Burma are roughly like this. As for what is usually called the rainy season, it only refers to whether it rains or not.

I advocate international openness and cooperation, with intermarriage as the center. Because all problems, physiology is the first. When physiology and bloodlines are assimilated, everything else will be different. In the past, Mr. Kang of the South China Sea recruited a poor scholar as his son-in-law, saying that this was also a method of communist regulation. This can be inferred from this. A friend told me that you advocate international intermarriage to harmonize all nations. Now, the Min and Cantonese people in Nanyang intermarry less because of language. However, in order to harmonize the Min and Cantonese people, we should also promote intermarriage between Min and Cantonese people, which is one way to combine the large group.

Nanyang is born of mixed races. The meaning of mixed races here is to express welcome, which is the opposite of what is often used in China to criticize. I have seen many children born to Burmese women and Westerners. They are very proficient in English. There are also many poor people, probably because their fathers died and they were displaced. Burmese women are intelligent and beautiful, so people from all countries often marry them. The attitude of Burmese women is probably better than that of Japanese women. Burmese people love beauty. Even the rural male laborers wear red shirts, full of rice fields, without raggedness and filth. Compared to the people north of the Huai River, they are far more elegant. Most people put flower pots on their doors, which is very elegant and clean. When female empowerment is popular, everyone will know how to love beauty, and the violent air of masculinity can be reduced day by day. I will use Burmese customs to predict it. Burma can be called a flower country, but why is China not as good? It is still possible south of the Huai River, but why is the north so degenerate?

And the past of its entire market course

The Whole Story of This Month's Cotton Delivery

Delivery price 33 and a half taels :: Quantity 36,100 *dan*

Recipients Long Companies :: Deliverers Han Gang and General Retailers

The situation of the marked cotton in December was sluggish at the beginning of the month. The world cotton industry was still in decline, buyers were scarce, the spot cotton trade was sluggish, the factories were saturated with printed cotton, and the need was completely stagnant. The majority were psychologically shorting, but the buyers were determined to go long as the standard was set high and there was a shortage of high-quality goods on the market, the Han Gang also seemed to go long, and the source was not prosperous. The short-selling retailers were in the majority, so the buyers turned short and their attitude was firm. In addition, the goods could not be inspected for several days at the end of the month due to customs closure, and the squeeze became more intense. The price at the beginning of the month was 31 taels and 7 or 8 *qian*, the lowest being 31 taels and 3 *qian* and a half, and the highest reaching 35 taels, exceeding the spot price on the market by more than 3 taels. This kind of situation was rare. Therefore, there was a storm on the upper day standard in January, and a request was made to the market to re-examine the standard. The standard remained in stalemate for two or three hours before the auction began. The resulting delivery price was 33 taels and 5 *qian*. The total delivery volume was 36,100 *dan*. The goods were Shaanxi fire machine, the recipients were long companies, and the deliverers were the Han Gang and retailers. Chairman Chiang Forgives China National Aviation Corporation

No Further Investigation into the Unauthorized Flight Incident

British Newspapers Recorded Falsehoods and Agreed to Correct Them

Before Chairman Chiang of the National Government left Wuhan to return to Nanjing, he had previously booked an aircraft from China National Aviation Corporation, intending to take the aircraft from Wuhan to Nanjing. On the morning of Chiang's departure from Wuhan, the aircraft flew away an hour earlier without authorization, resulting in a temporary change to take a warship. This matter was detailed in the Hankou telegrams a few days ago. When Chairman Chiang came to Shanghai, he saw that the local English-language *Great Evening News* reported that Chiang had arrested Mr. Kirk, an employee of China National Aviation Corporation, for this matter, and stated that the company's branch office in Wuhan had been closed. This was obviously inconsistent with the facts. Song Ziwen was ordered to negotiate. Yesterday morning, Song entrusted Liu Yunfang of the Foreign Affairs Office to report the denial to the *Great Evening News* and ordered a correction. The newspaper agreed to comply. It is heard that Chairman Chiang was magnanimous and did not investigate the unauthorized departure of the aircraft. However, he expressed dissatisfaction with the company's negligence. Yesterday morning, Liu personally went to China National Aviation Corporation at No. 3 Guangdong Road and invited Mr. Hamilton, the company's Western manager, to Song's office to accept questioning. Song met at the Guohuo Bank on Hankou Road, inquired about the process, and ordered the company to formally apologize in writing.

Port Authority Handover Yesterday

The Municipal Government Port Authority, by order of the Executive Yuan, has temporarily suspended its establishment and, according to the order of the Municipal Government, will be closed by the end of this year. All its functions will be taken over by the Bureau of Public Utilities, the Bureau of Land Affairs, and the Bureau of Public Works. Details have been previously reported. Yesterday, the Port Authority completed its closure, and the Municipal Government, together with the three bureaus, went to take over. The details are recorded as follows:

Takeover Situation: Yesterday at 10:00 AM, personnel from the Municipal Government, the Bureau of Land Affairs, the Bureau of Public Works, and the Bureau of Public Utilities went to take over. The Municipal Government was represented by Qi Xuan, the head of the First Section, who, along with staff members, took over the files and equipment of the Port Authority's First Section. The head of the Port Authority's First Section and others handed over the items one by one. The Bureau of Land Affairs sent staff members such as Sheng Kai to take over matters related to the management of the shoreline, which were handed over by the Port Authority's Second Section. The Bureau of Public Utilities, led by Secretary Xu Yuanfang, along with staff members, took over the wharf management office and the sand dredging boat registration office. The director of the management office, Xu Shipu, accompanied them to the Bund to hand over the operations. The Bureau of Public Works was represented by Tan Wenqing, the head of the First Section, who led staff members to take over the dyke works office and the dredging of waterways, which were handed over by the Port Authority's Second Section.

However, the sand dredging boat registration office is located far away in Wusong, and the dyke works office is also in Gaoqiao. The Bureau of Public Utilities and the Bureau of Public Works were unable to reach these locations yesterday, so the takeover is scheduled for today.

Renaming of Two Offices: The Wusong sand dredging boat registration office and the Nanshi wharf management office, which will be taken over by the Bureau of Public Utilities, will be renamed the Shanghai Wharf and Warehouse Management Office and the Wusong Shipping Office after the takeover. The office locations will remain unchanged.

Staff Placement: Now that the Port Authority has completed its closure, the salaries for the staff this month were distributed by Director Xi Dingmo yesterday morning. Regarding the placement of staff members, personnel from the sand dredging boat registration office, the dyke works office, and the Nanshi wharf management office will remain in their positions as usual. Other staff members within the Port Authority will be assigned to various bureaus for employment, depending on the circumstances. Director Xi Dingmo has already been appointed as a Municipal Government Advisor. It is reported that those who cannot be placed will have their severance pay requested from the Municipal Government.
