Judicial Yuan Interpretation of Tenancy Relationship

Regarding the issue of renovating houses

In recent years, disputes between landlords and tenants have arisen frequently in this city regarding tenancy issues. Cases of coercion and eviction often occur. Landlords, on the other hand, argue that their property rights should not be compromised. As a result, these issues often become social legal problems. According to a report from the Xin Sheng News Agency in Beijing, the Judicial Yuan recently issued instruction No. 1177 on December 23, 1920, to the Jiangsu Higher Court, requesting an interpretation of a case where a tenant renovated a rented house at their own expense without setting a specific term. The question was whether the tenant could be ordered to move out at any time. This has significant implications for rented houses in this city. The hypothetical scenario and instructions are excerpted below:

Hypothetical scenario: Party A rents a house to open a large-scale store. Because the original building was simple and dilapidated, Party A obtained Party B's consent and invested their own funds to renovate several Western-style houses on the land, totaling approximately 50,000 yuan in construction costs and 18,000 yuan in miscellaneous expenses. Party A continued to rent the property. However, the contract did not specify a lease term. After only a few years, a business in the same neighborhood, whose landlord was also Party B, offered a large amount of money to induce Party B to force Party A to move out. They secretly agreed that the business would invest a certain amount in Party B's business. Party B used the pretext of self-use to force Party A to move out. The handling of real estate is the owner's right, and tenants cannot be allowed to occupy it forever. However, landlords who forcibly evict tenants must also consider the facts and the regulations in Section 5 of Article 230 of the old Civil Code on obligations regarding lease agreements. Protection of the rights of the tenant is particularly thorough. Article 450 of the newly promulgated Civil Code states, "If no time limit is set, either party may terminate the contract at any time, but if there is a custom that favors the tenant, the custom shall prevail." This also takes into account the interests of the tenant. Party A has already spent a large sum of money to renovate the new house. After only a few years of completion, they are being asked to move out, and the cost of their entire business and house construction will be completely sacrificed. This not only violates custom (in Shanghai, there is a custom that landlords cannot force tenants to move out within ten years if the tenant has invested their own funds to build the house) but also goes against reason. Self-use must also have necessary circumstances. Merely investing in someone else's existing store is a joint venture, which is different from self-use. If this becomes a precedent, the tenant's entire business will not be protected, and it will harm society. Weighing the law and the facts, we request the court to provide a fair interpretation as soon as possible.

Judicial Yuan's response: Having received the case, we have forwarded it to the Supreme Court to prepare a proposed interpretation and submit it for review. It states that if a tenant invests in renovating a rented house and the landlord is aware of the situation but does not express any objection, and if the lease contract does not specify a term, the landlord may terminate the contract at any time. However, if there is no special agreement regarding the renovation costs, the landlord shall compensate the tenant for the existing increased value of the house when the lease relationship ends (refer to Article 431 of the Civil Code). If the lease contract does not specify a term, according to Article 450, paragraph 2 of the Civil Code, if there is a local custom regarding the termination of the contract that restricts the landlord and favors the tenant, the custom shall prevail. Having carefully reviewed this, we find no discrepancies. This order is hereby issued for your information.

Naval Department Orders Ship Owners to Add Gun Emplacements to Ships

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Adds Four Seas Liners

Made in the country to show promotion

The local shipping companies received a dispatch from the Ministry of Communications forwarded from the Naval Department, stating that merchant ships can be used as auxiliary naval vessels in times of war, which is a common practice in various countries. When constructing these ships, it is necessary to prepare for the installation of artillery, so the hull must be strong and the speed must be increased to be applicable. Although the construction is convenient for navigation, the cost of shipbuilding will inevitably increase. Traditionally, the government provides subsidies according to the price, so that rights and obligations are equally divided. Recently, state-owned merchant ships have been used to meet the temporary needs of the navy, such as the Queen's Wheel of England and the Presidential Wheel of the United States. This demonstrates the intention of your ministry to revitalize navigation and prepare to reclaim navigation rights. At present, various countries have signed international conventions on maritime safety, stipulating that old ships must be modified and new ships must meet construction procedures. As the trend of the times, all countries believe that it is more convenient to build new ships than to modify old ones. China's shipping industry is just emerging, and it is very important for your ministry to add new ships at this time, which is enough to make a new impression. It seems that we should not buy what others discard. The two shipyards, Jiangnan and Mawei, under the jurisdiction of our ministry, built many ships of more than 10,000 tons for the US government during the European War. Now we have ordered the factories to prepare the shipbuilding procedures in detail. Domestic shipbuilding can be labor-saving and inexpensive, and can compete internationally. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's north-south routes need to put in place four new ships of 3,000 tons each. This type of coastal ship is most suitable for 3,000 tons. Although the bureau is state-owned, it is a commercial enterprise. For temporary military purposes, the Ministry will discuss subsidy methods for all increased construction costs. If agreed, the Ministry will order the departments to design, draw, and estimate prices, and prepare a plan, which will be discussed by the two ministries, aiming to proceed in a timely manner, so that the military and business can benefit.

British Police Arrest Indian Trespassers

Indian Youth League Protests

Da Wan Bao reported that an Indian named Xin Nanxin escaped from the isolation ward of the police station yesterday (28th) and fled to Zhabei. He was arrested by the Chinese police. As of this afternoon (29th), he is still detained at the Zhabei Police Station. According to personnel from the Public Concession Police Station, they will ask the Public Security Bureau to extradite him for interrogation today. Xin had previously been arrested with another Indian, Ka Taixin, on the 3rd of this month for distributing leaflets at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Qiujiang Road. On the 5th, he was sent to the British Police Court for trial. Ka pleaded not guilty in court and stated the justice of the Indian people's call for independence. Xin remained silent. At that time, Xin was charged with three counts: drunkenness and disturbing public order, privately possessing a pistol, and distributing inflammatory writings. In addition to the first two counts, which were sentenced to imprisonment, the third count was still pending transfer to the Office of the Provincial Judge for trial. Recently, Xin became ill in prison and was transferred to an isolation hospital for treatment. He took the opportunity to go to the bathroom at 6:00 AM on the 28th and escaped through the window. He fled to Zhabei and took refuge in an Indian church. When detectives from the Public Concession, accompanied by officers from the Public Security Bureau, went to arrest him, the people in the church were agitated and difficult to offend. Later, the Chinese police arrested him near Zhenru. The Indian Youth League has written to the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to protest against the five British police officers and two Indian informants from the Public Concession, who, without Chinese police officers, armed themselves and entered the league's office at 241 Baoxing Road, drawing weapons. They then went to the Indian church to arrest Xin Nanxin. It is claimed that they used guns to threaten Xin Nanxin with handcuffs and then tried to handcuff those who were campaigning to restore Xin's freedom. The Indian comrades closed the church door and locked the five people indoors, forcing them to release the illegally arrested comrades before letting them go. At that time, two British men outside the door ordered the five people inside to shoot and kill the comrades. Not long after, three Chinese policemen went to arrest Xin Nanxin, who was immediately arrested without resistance, because we live in the Chinese district and of course recognize Chinese law. The letter also requested that Xin not be extradited to the Concession Police Station.

New Year's Holiday for Various Agencies

Post Office: It is reported that the local post office will be closed for five days from December 31st to January 4th by order. Therefore, the office hours are regulated, except that the office will be closed all day on New Year's Day, and the rest of the days will be handled as on Sundays. Furthermore, fearing that there may be a backlog of letters, special deliveries will be made on the evening of the 31st to deliver as many mails as possible within the year for the convenience of the public.

Commodity Inspection Bureau: The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry received an order from the ministry to transfer the telegram from the Executive Yuan, stating that the Central Government has decided to change the holiday date for the National Calendar New Year to five days, from December 31st to January 4th. All sectors should not close during the Lunar New Year in order to promote the National Calendar and change people's habits. After receiving the order, the bureau immediately obeyed and will be closed for five days from tomorrow (31st) to January 4th, and will stop reporting inspections. All staff and merchants have been notified accordingly.

Municipal Council: The Shanghai Municipal Council's New Year's holiday has now been set from New Year's Day to the 3rd, for a New Year's holiday. The 4th, Sunday, is a regular holiday, and the office will resume normal work from the 5th.

Money Exchange Industry Changes Holiday Dates

The money exchange industry will finalize the year-end accounts of the National Calendar year and extend the payment of loans to February 15th. As such, the money house's accounts for this year must be finalized by February 15th. However, the Money Exchange Industry Association previously published a notice of the holiday dates in the newspaper. The committee resolved yesterday that there would be some changes. The New Year holidays are four days from New Year's Day. Business will resume as usual on the 5th. As for February 15th, the last day for sorting out unfinished matters after the settlement of accounts, there will be three days of holidays on the 16th, 17th, and 18th. However, at the request of the various Chinese banks, all year-end collections and payments must be processed on the 16th. Therefore, the receipt and payment of transactions to the same industry and banks will continue to be processed. However, the end point for the settlement of accounts with customers will still be February 15th. In this case, the receipt and payment will be handled as usual on the 16th, and the business will be closed on the 17th and 18th for internal planning. Business will resume as usual on February 19th.

Completion of the May 30th Massacre Family Association

And Report on Income and Expenditure Accounts

The May 30th Massacre Victims' Family Association previously requested the Municipal Council, through directors Yu Qiaqing and others, to allocate all the 150,000 yuan of compensation funds to the board of directors, together with the Family Association, to distribute to the families of the victims of the May 30th Massacre. By the 15th of last month, all procedures were completed, and the income and expenditure accounts were also closed at the same time. For the sake of solemnity, the board of directors entrusted accountant Jiang Xinzhao to examine and certify all the accounts. The examination was completed the day before yesterday, and accountant Jiang issued a certificate and an audit report, which were sent to the board of directors and forwarded to the party and government agencies of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Interior, and the Ministry of Finance for record. A summary of the income and expenditure accounts was also printed separately and distributed to the families for inspection. The Family Association announced the closure of the association immediately after the procedures were completed. The board of directors believed that the income and expenditure accounts of this case, which is related to the Chinese and foreign public, should be publicly reported. The detailed income and expenditure accounts are recorded below: (Income) The Municipal Council allocated all the 150,000 yuan of compensation funds; (Expenditure) Compensation funds for the families of 55 victims of the massacre were 74,500 yuan (including 24 martyrs who died, each receiving 2,000 yuan of compensation, 28 lightly injured, each receiving 500 yuan, one severely injured and disabled, 2,500 yuan, and 5,000 yuan each for Chen and Hu, the two representatives who were disabled, totaling the above amount); 35,000 yuan was paid back to Yu, the chairman of the former Chamber of Commerce, to repay the advance payment, and 1,710 yuan was paid for the expenses incurred over the years; 20,000 yuan was paid to Cheng Xiechun, director of the May 30th Cemetery, to repay the advance payment for the construction of the cemetery; 2,825 yuan was paid for the public expenses and advance payment of the staff of the association over the years; 2,794 yuan and 59 cents were paid for the various expenses of the association (including 20 yuan and 2 cents for the association utensils, 25 yuan and 22 cents and 2 mils for stationery, 236 yuan and 51 cents and 3 mils for rickshaw, 231 yuan for rent, 330 yuan for salary, 540 yuan and 52 cents and 6 mils for food, 6 yuan and 57 cents and 5 mils for postage, 31 yuan and 74 cents for newspapers, 153 yuan and 26 cents and 4 mils for miscellaneous items, 175 yuan and 60 cents for advertising, 23 yuan and 50 cents for photography, 555 yuan and 60 cents for lawyer fees, 350 yuan for the Luo case settlement fee, and 100 yuan for accountant consulting fee, totaling the above amount); 100 yuan was paid for the closing expenses of the association, 100 yuan for the audit fee, and 170 yuan and 41 cents for the report root project newspaper fee, etc. The above items totaled 137,200 yuan. The remaining 12,800 yuan in cash and the interest to be paid are still kept by Director Yu Qiaqing as a permanent fund for the May 30th Cemetery.

The Government Silk Industry Requests Attention to the Raw Material Wild Silk Tax Rate

The Fu Silk Guild sent a telegram to Zhang, the Director of the Customs Department of the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, stating that the Fu silk produced in Shandong, Andong, and Henan is woven purely with wild silk and is sold exclusively to foreign countries. It is one of the exported native products. Recently, the wild silk material produced in Liaoning and Ning has been absorbed by the eastern neighbor, accounting for six or seven tenths of the total amount. They rely on their low export tax from South Manchuria to compete with our country in sales to Europe and the United States, and have already been almost completely taken away. It is requested that the Ministry carefully consider the tax rate, reduce the tax rate on raw material wild silk domestically, and appropriately increase the export tax. It is also requested that the export of Fu silk be exempted from tax, according to the tea leaf precedent. In addition to sending a special letter of request, this telegram is sent. The Shanghai Shandong Henan Silk Industry Office respectfully states.

The 171st

The Municipal Government held its 171st Municipal Government meeting on December 12, 1920. The Fujian Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai yesterday received a telegram from Zhang Zhen, Brigade Commander and Commander of the Anti-Communist Frontline, Yang Fengnian, as follows: "To the Fujian Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, all newspaper offices, all levels of party departments, all societies, all chambers of commerce, and all charitable organizations: Western Fujian and more than ten counties have been brutally ravaged by the Communist bandits. Disputes Involving China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Vessels All Concluded

Tonghua Incident Resolved

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Tonghua vessel had seamen beaten by workers and crew members arrested in Qingkou, and dockworkers went on strike. These incidents were reported in this newspaper. Now, it is learned that the company telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government, requesting the Ganyu County Magistrate to release the arrested crew members to maintain operations and facilitate transportation. After two telegrams urging action, Haizhou has now replied, stating that the Ganyu County has concluded the investigation of this conflict. Both the seamen and the workers were injured. The county has ordered the Tonghua vessel to pay a fine of 300 yuan to be used as medical expenses for the eight injured workers. At the same time, the labor union was ordered to resume work as usual from today. Both parties agreed, and the Tonghua case has come to a temporary conclusion. The arrested crew members and the headmen of the stokers and watermen were released yesterday and returned to the ship.

Haiyan Case Adjudicated

On April 25 of this year, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Haiyan vessel sank three wheat barges and drowned a boatman at the Jinliyuan Wharf. The victims filed a lawsuit in court, and the owner of the Haiyan vessel specially hired lawyer Wang Naimu as defense counsel. The case has now been concluded. The charge of manslaughter brought by the victims was dismissed, but a fine of 500 yuan was imposed for negligence in business operations. The judgment has been delivered, and it is reported that an appeal is planned to argue for the cancellation of the fine.

Replacement of Crew Members

In order to rectify the qualifications of crew members, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company believes that all members on various vessels who do not have certificates from the Ministry of Communications are unqualified. After investigation by the shipping department, it was found that one member in the navigation department and eight members in the engine department did not have certificates from the ministry. They have been ordered to resign, and the company has appointed members with certificates from the ministry to fill their positions from among the reserve navigators and engineers. It was heard yesterday that the nine members who were dismissed have registered with the Ministry of Communications and applied for certificates for commercial vessel personnel.

Lide Oil Factory Reopens Yesterday

Social Affairs Bureau Suspends Labor Union Activities

In November, short-term workers at the Lide Oil Factory in Tanzhiwan, Zhabei, demanded a wage increase without success, resulting in a labor dispute. The factory director, Liu Changyin, decided to temporarily close the factory due to excessive losses caused by the workers' slowdown. Fortunately, the Social Affairs Bureau mediated and decided to increase the wages of each short-term worker by one yuan, and then work continued. Before a month had passed, long-term workers went on strike together with those aware of the issue because of the rice subsidy issue. The factory could not withstand the losses and announced a shutdown again on the 18th, while applying to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for fair mediation. It is reported that the Bureau has approved the factory to dismiss the seven workers who initiated the labor unrest as a punishment, and ordered them to start work again soon. Furthermore, because the factory's labor union had not been re-elected for three years, it was deemed necessary to thoroughly reorganize it. Therefore, the labor union was ordered to hand in its seal and license and temporarily suspend activities, pending reorganization. It is also said that since receiving the approval from the Social Affairs Bureau, the factory reopened yesterday, but the remaining long-term and short-term workers have not yet returned to work.

Municipal Health Bureau Pays Attention to the Mixed Sale of Diseased Livestock Meat in Concessions

The Municipal Health Bureau has assigned qualified veterinarians to inspect livestock and the sale of livestock meat in the city. Any diseased or dead livestock or diseased meat found will be detained and sent to rendering plants to be rendered into oil for industrial use, in order to prevent harm to the health of citizens. Subsidies will also be issued to the owners of the items, so as to express condolences. However, if there is private slaughtering or private sale of diseased or dead livestock meat, once discovered, the Public Security Bureau will be requested to impose severe penalties to deter others from following suit. Because the Health Department of the Public Concession has already followed the urging and carried out post-slaughter inspection, but nothing has been heard about how to dispose of diseased or dead livestock and diseased meat, the Bureau has specifically written to the Health Department of the Public Works Department of the Concession to inquire about disposal methods, and informed them that if there is no proper disposal method, the diseased or dead livestock from the racetrack dairy farm or slaughterhouse can be ordered to be sent to the oil rendering plant in the south of the city for rendering, and subsidies will be issued to prevent mixed slaughter and sale, and to emphasize the safety of meat products consumed by citizens within the boundaries. The Municipal Council of the Public Concession then replied, stating that it was deeply appreciative of the suggestions of the Municipal Health Bureau, and that the Municipal Council was also well aware that the current disposal of dead livestock was not entirely appropriate, and that it was currently carefully considering ways to improve it as soon as possible. However, in the shortest possible time, the current disposal methods could not be changed. The Municipal Health Bureau believed that the current improper disposal methods had already been reported in the past, and that it was said that there were no changes that could be made, allowing the sale of diseased and dead meat to be sold openly, abandoning the responsibility of maintaining public health. A further letter was sent urging that improvements be made as soon as possible, and that there should be no collusion with unscrupulous meat merchants to allow them to privately transport diseased meat into the jurisdiction of this city for mixed sale, so as to fulfill their responsibilities and emphasize the health of citizens.

Lease of Stalls in Baxianqiao Vegetable Market

Article 1: The Municipal Council will solicit bids for leasing vegetable market stalls in the second half of each December. Article 2: The stalls in the vegetable market are classified by category and area. The location of each type of stall is detailed in the vegetable market map attached to these bylaws. Article 3: Each stall has a number, and the lease term is one full year, from January 1 to December 31. Article 4: Each stall will be leased through auction, with the highest bidder winning the bid. Article 5: The bid price refers to the monthly rent for each stall, and the minimum amount must be the standard rent in Article 11 below. Article 6: No one may bid on more than two stalls of the same type. Article 7: Bidding on behalf of others is not allowed. Article 8: The winning bidder must pay one quarter's rent on the spot. The rent for each stall must also be paid in advance on a quarterly basis thereafter. Article 9: If a stall becomes vacant during the year, the Municipal Council may assign it to the applicant at any time. Article 10: If the winning bidder fails to pay the quarterly rent before the 15th of the first month of each quarter, they will lose the right to rent the stall. Article 11: The standard rent for each stall is as follows: Stalls downstairs: 6 taels of silver per stall per month. Stalls upstairs: (A) Vegetable stalls: 3 taels of silver per stall per month. (B) Food stalls: 15 yuan per stall per month. Ordered by Director Fuller. (Note: The bidding date will be determined separately. To see the detailed map, please go to the Director's Office of this bureau.)

A Glimpse into the Contents of the Central Society

Aimed at Improving Society

The Central Society is located at No. 150 Weihaiwei Road, west of Moore Road, occupying more than 40 squares of space in a three-story building. The east side is the library and the bathroom. The lower floor of the building houses the barber shop and the consumer cooperative department, with the dining hall in the middle. The second floor is the social room, conference room, ladies' lounge, and Chinese kitchen. The third floor is the dormitory for members, the recreation room, the Go room, and the gym. In the middle is the office of the executive officers and the recreation room, equipped with two billiard tables, ping-pong tables, and chess tables. Above is a platform from which one can see the scenery of western Shanghai in the distance, all in sight. Looking at the entire building, it is extremely magnificent. The interior decoration is also simple but beautiful. There are currently more than 300 members, including artists, entrepreneurs, bankers, famous lawyers, accountants, and university professors in Shanghai, all of whom are included in the network. They gather middle-class people in one place, aiming to improve society. The internal organization includes a board of directors, with Wu Jingxiong, Chen Fangzhi, Xu Xinliu, Cen Dezhang, Yu Fengshao, De Bihua, and Li Gufan as the seven directors; an economic committee, with Shen Yuqing, Xu Guangde, Chen Chunzhong, Xu Zhiyi, and Dai Ailu as the five members; a club committee, with Jiang Xiaohe, Zheng Jingshan, Pan Gongbi, Zheng Yanzuo, Zeng Guangqing, Lu Dingkui, and Yu Zongjiao as the seven members; a library committee, with Sheng Tongsun, Chen Weiqing, Hua Runquan, Xu Zhimo, and Zhang Jiefang as the five members; and a publishing committee, with Zhu Qinglai, Yu Songhua, Lu Xirong, Ge Gongzhen, and Wei Bozhen as the five members. The daily management of the society is handled by the general secretary, the administrative secretary, and the accounting secretary, who handle matters in groups, with clear regulations. There are also two research committees, the Consumer Cooperative Department and the Customs Improvement Department, which are currently being organized. It is expected that the behind-the-scenes work will be carried out in an orderly manner. This is a general overview of the Central Society, and the society's prohibition of gambling and prostitution is a clear distinction from general clubs in Shanghai. It is reported that it has been decided to open on New Year's Day and welcome visitors from all walks of life.

Shipping Industry Will Not Close for the New Year

On New Year's Day of the 20th year of the Republic of China, most transportation industries will not close. (1) (Yangtze River Route) The Sanbei Company, a Chinese company, and the Changxing Wheel, as well as the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiangyu Wheel, will all depart for Hankou on the evening of New Year's Day. The Ning Shao Company's Ning Shao Wheel will depart for Hankou on the 2nd. (2) (Shanghai-Ningbo Route) The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xin Jiangtian Wheel and the Sanbei Company's Ningxing Wheel will depart from Shanghai to Ningbo on New Year's Day. On the same day, the Ning Shao Company's Xin Ningshao Wheel and the foreign company Taikoo Company's Xin Beijing Wheel will depart from Ningbo for Shanghai. (3) (Tongyang Route) The Shanghai-Yangzhou routes operated by Dada and Datong Companies will be closed for two days on the 1st and 2nd. (4) (Shanghai-Wenzhou Route) All shipping companies operating between Shanghai and Wenzhou Kanmen will operate as usual.

Today at 1:00 PM

The year-end bonuses for employees of the Shanghai Ordnance Factory were previously set by the Ordnance Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs and issued until the 18th year. Revisions to Truck Donation Rates

Divided into Three Levels of Collection

The Shanghai Public Security Bureau approved the letter from the Public Utilities Bureau yesterday, stating that the donation rates for trucks in this city in the past were poorly defined and troublesome. Now, after consultation with the Finance Bureau, it has been submitted to the Municipal Government and approved to be divided into three levels: Tiger cars will be in the first class, with a monthly donation of one yuan; box trucks, flour trucks, oil trucks, firewood trucks, etc. will be in the second class, with a monthly donation of three yuan; and flatbed trucks will be in the third class, with a monthly donation of five yuan. In addition, numbers will be re-assigned, and new license plates will be re-issued. It is scheduled to begin processing from December 25 of this year. The relevant new license plates and licenses are being sent for inspection and re-distribution to the relevant departments for implementation. Any violations of these regulations will be punished according to the regulations. Director Yuan has ordered his subordinates to comply.

New Wall Calendar Published

Published by the Astronomical Institute of the Academia Sinica

The Astronomical Institute of the National Academia Sinica has been publishing a weekly calendar every year since 1929. The material is rich, the printing is exquisite, and it has long been popular. It is now heard that the 1931 weekly calendar has also been published. The format is more novel, and the content is even more complete. Each week has one page, with a five-color image printed on the upper part, with a simple explanation. The lower part contains the sequence of days in the week, the seven luminaries, moon phases, star phases, and commemorative days. The remaining space contains short biographies of Chinese and Western astronomers. Each book sells for one yuan. Local sales offices are the Wenming Bookstore on Nanjing Road, the Commercial Press on Qipan Street, and the Publication Exchange of the Academia Sinica at 331 Avenue Albert. Inland mail orders can be directly sent to the Astronomical Institute in Gulou, Nanjing.

The Trial of Hu Die's Lawsuit Against the Ling Bao Newspaper

The Eloquent Arguments of Both Lawyers

The Verdict: A Fine of Three Hundred Yuan

Lu Yifang Appeals

Hu Die, a female actor in the Mingxing Film Company, had a dispute with her fiancé, Lin Xuehuai, over the cancellation of their engagement. Lu Yifang, the editor of the three-day Ling Bao newspaper, published an article entitled "Hu Lin Divorce Record," which stated that Hu had been a prostitute and relied on others to become a small star. Hu believed that the newspaper intentionally defamed her reputation and instructed lawyer Zhan Jifeng to send a letter requesting a correction. However, the Ling Bao newspaper attached the phrase "Everything Heard is Recorded" to the correction and published a photo of Zhu Fei, a male actor in the Mingxing Film Company, in the next issue, with the words "A Key Figure in the Xue Die Divorce." Hu further believed that this was a deliberate attempt to damage her reputation and filed a criminal self-accusation with the Special District Court. It had been summoned and the defendant Lu Yifang was ordered to pay a bail of five hundred yuan to guarantee his appearance for further interrogation. This was detailed in the previous report. Strict Search of Cars in the Desolate Areas of West Shanghai

A Method to Prevent Kidnapping

Wang Section Chief of the First Branch of the Sixth District of Northwest Shanghai, in view of the recent major kidnapping cases in various parts of Shanghai, has repeatedly appeared. The jurisdiction of this district is vast, desolate and secluded. Sometimes bandits hide or bandit cars pass through. Although he has ordered all his subordinate branches to send police to conduct strict searches, it is still not a thorough solution. It is now heard that Wang Section Chief, in order to find out that the kidnapped car, or is hired to the company, or is the car of the victim, in order to be easy to break, since the previous day, strictly ordered各分所, regardless of day or night, to go to Hongqiao Road 大西路 罗别根路 林肯路 and other roads to send police to conduct strict inspections, for the cars to and from, the driver's license must be checked, and the number must be copied, one side and then a detailed search for a week, before you can pass.

The Wife of a Trackman at the South Station Gave Birth to a Monster

Eyes Growing on Forehead and Emitting Green Light

Two Bloody Horns Growing on the Top of Head

Squeaking and Gurgling After Falling to the Ground

Drowned in Hot Water by Family Members

Chen A'si, a resident at No. 86 Zhangjiazhai, west of the South Railway Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, is 30 years old and a native of Suzhou. He has been working as a trackman at the South Railway Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway for many years. He married a woman named Cheng, also from Suzhou, who is 31 years old. The couple is known for their harmony and has not yet had children. However, in the second month of the lunar calendar this year, Chen's wife became pregnant. At around 12 o'clock the night before, she suddenly went into labor and gave birth to a monster. It was about one foot and five inches long, with a flat head and eyes growing on its forehead. The eyeballs were very large, round, and green, resembling cat's eyes. Two bloody horns also emitting green light grew on the top of its head. It had hair on the back of its head, and its mouth, ears, nose were all complete, but its mouth was large and had teeth. Its hands were very long, reaching below its knees, and its calves had testicles but no core. After being born, it could run and jump and make squeaking and gurgling noises. When the pregnant woman heard this, she was greatly shocked. Chen A'si immediately called over many neighbors to come and see. All who saw it were amazed and said it was a monster, which would bring harm and no benefit. Some said it would grow up in the wind and might be dangerous. Opinions were divided. Later, Chen A'si drowned it in hot water and threw the strange corpse into a small river in Yangqi Huining Road, west of the station.

Three Ships Run Aground on the Yangtze River in One Day

Water Level Drops:: Navigation Difficult

The Xing Shi Wheel of the Xing Shi Sanbei Company was leased by the Transportation Department for service. Last month, its engine was damaged in Pukou. The company sent technicians to Beijing to repair it. This time, the ship was sailing to Hankou. Due to the large drop in the river water, the Xing Shi Wheel ran aground on a shoal six Hua Li downstream of Bujia Town due to the receding tide. At that time, it was impossible to leave the shoal. Both the Shanghai and Hankou bureaus have been urgently telegraphed to send a wheel to tow.

The Bei Fu, of the Northern Shipping Company, which usually sails along the coast line, was carrying salt from Haizhou to Hankou this time. Unexpectedly, the ship ran aground near the Xiaogushan lighthouse ship. This area has hidden reefs and shallow sands, making it the most difficult for wheels to navigate. The Bei Fu ship mistakenly sailed onto the shoal, and the ship also ran aground. It is not yet possible to leave the area and a ship must be sent to tow it. It is not yet known whether the bottom of the ship has been damaged.

The Da Zhong wheel of the Heng'an Company in this port had a telegram from Shanghai yesterday, saying that the ship ran aground about six miles downstream of Anqing at a place called Yaojiawan. It was found that the river surface in this area was newly measured. The Da Zhong wheel ran aground because it was not clear about the river channel. The Shanghai Bureau is now trying to send a ship to rescue it. Whether there is any damage will only be clear after it is out of danger. Recently, the Yangtze River waterway has been shrinking day by day, so sailing is very difficult. Three ships were wrecked in one day, which is indeed unfortunate news for the Yangtze River.

Fierce Battle Between Group Police and Bandits in He Xiang Bridge

One Bandit Child Killed

Two Bandit Boats Intercepted

In Zhongda Bridge River Port, at the junction of Shangsong, two counties in Hexiang Bridge, Minhang Town, under the jurisdiction of the county, at about 3 pm the other day (28th), two bandit boats suddenly came, with more than 20 men and women on board. Chen, the leader of the county's first district security group stationed there, immediately notified Yuan, the patrol officer of the second squad of the first district of the water police, and led the group police to rush to encircle and capture. Unexpectedly, the bandits opened fire and refused to be arrested. The group police also returned fire. For a time, bullets flew across, as if facing a formidable enemy. After about an hour, the bandit forces were unable to support and began to flee towards the newly built Beihui Road. One bandit child over ten years old was shot and killed on the spot, and two bullets and two bandit boats were seized.

News Report on a Dispute Over Found Money

A Hubei boy, Su Baogen, residing at No. 331 Yat Road, found a package of paper money totaling over one thousand yuan at the entrance of the Universal Theatre on East-West Huade Road at 4:00 PM on the 26th of this month. He took it home, and his neighbors, upon learning of this, attempted to share the money but failed. They arranged a negotiation at the Yile Tian Tea House on Nanjing Road the day before yesterday afternoon. The Hongkou police station was informed and dispatched detective Wang Runhe and a Western detective in secret. They arrested five Ningbo men, Lu A'ding, Shen Shoufang, Wu Changhua, Wang Jihou, and Gao Cailin, and detained them at the police station. This matter was already reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the Special District Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, stated the facts of the case, saying that the paper money handed over to the police station by the plaintiff, after inspection by the inspector, was actually one thousand and five yuan, and is now stored at the police station. However, it is speculated that the owner may not be a legitimate person, because the paper money package was very dirty, etc. Then, Fu A'long, a relative of the boy, testified that the defendants, upon learning of the money, intended to extort five hundred yuan but failed, so they arranged the negotiation at the tea house, hence the arrest. Attorney Fan Gang was retained to defend them. After the boy Su Baogen and his mother Su Liu testified, they were questioned. The defendants stammered and denied the charges, seeking judgment. Judge Xiao Xieffen verified the confessions and sentenced the five defendants, Lu A'ding and others, to 30 days of detention each, with a two-year suspended sentence. The one thousand and five yuan will be kept pending claims. The police lawyer Zhang, upon hearing the verdict, stated that the police station disagreed with the suspended sentence and would appeal. During the appeal period, the defendants will remain in custody. The court approved.

Chinese Helper on Japanese Fishing Boat Dies Tragically

Leg Bones Broken by Wire

Body Collected by Friend

Japanese fishing boats frequently cross the sea to illegally catch fish, despite strong opposition from our country's fishing industry. However, their boat construction is superior to ours, and they use machines for fishing, hiring Chinese as helpers. Recently, the Japanese fishing boat Takekyu No. 1 came to the waters outside the mouth of the Yangtze River in our country to fish. At 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, when the boat was working near Huaniaoshan Island, Chen Jingcai, a Chinese helper on the boat, was operating the motor winch. The wire attached to the winch suddenly became tangled. Chen kicked it with his foot, but inadvertently his foot became entangled in the wire, which wrapped around it four times. By the time others stopped the winch, Chen's leg bones had already been broken. He immediately fell and died. The boat owner, Tamachito, ordered the boat to sail into Shanghai at 10:00 AM today, temporarily docking at the Xiang Sheng Iron Factory in Lujiazui, Pudong. He also sent someone to report to the Water Police Station. The police chief ordered detective Cheng Yongnian to rush to the scene and bring the body back to the police station. In the afternoon, it was transferred to the autopsy room of the Tongren Fuyuan Hall Rescue Bureau, pending an autopsy by the local court. It is reported that the deceased was 26 years old and from Rongcheng County, Dengzhou Prefecture, Shandong Province. His body will be collected by his friend Bao Wenyi.

Letter to the Editor

To the Editor: We recently read a news item in your newspaper's "Local News" column on the 26th regarding the Ministry of Finance's abolishment of the Jiangsu Bureau of Official Property for Land Reclamation, which stated that the case was presented to the provincial government by the people of Changshu and Jiangyin counties, who requested amendments and reforms to the bureau's various tax policies that harmed the country and the people, and that the provincial government approved this and forwarded it to the Ministry of Finance for review. The Jiangsu Official Property for Land Reclamation has been in operation for more than ten years and is at the end of its rope. The Ministry of Finance's explicit order to handle the results is purely to reduce the scope and save expenses, initiated by the Ministry itself. The later statements are inconsistent with the facts. We hereby send this letter to request a correction to avoid misunderstandings. Sincerely, Jiangsu Bureau of Official Property for Land Reclamation.

Grounds

Championship - Sigh

The clanging bell broke the silence of the entire school. The classroom doors opened, and students poured out like a tide. Some jumped out of the windows to avoid the crowding. Everyone's face showed a look of joy, probably because there was an important championship competition in the school today, and they could enjoy a feast for the eyes.

I was arranging books in the dormitory when the door was pushed open with a "ya" sound. The most mischievous Zhen walked in.

"Ah, don't study anymore! There are still two weeks until the exam. Today we have a football match with the sixth grade for the championship. Come and help us cheer!"

I looked at him and couldn't help but laugh. He was wearing a sheepskin robe inside out, a paper hat on his head, and a white cloth flag in his hand with the words "Fifth Grade Cheerleading Squad" written on it.

"Zhen, are you the captain of the cheerleading squad?" I asked.

"No, they elected me to do it. Don't waste time. Come with me!"

"You go first. I still have two math problems to solve. I'll come when I'm done."

":::::: Sitting across from me, Qin, was absentmindedly reading a book, seemingly not hearing Zhen's request. "Qin is a hardworking student. He won't join our foolishness. Xin, don't break your promise. Come when you're done with the math problems," Zhen said and turned to leave.

"Such a grown-up person, still so foolish," Qin suddenly looked up and said to me.

"Um:::::" I couldn't think of a suitable answer for a moment and had to respond vaguely.

I originally planned to watch the soccer game after finishing the math problems, but after Qin said that, I felt a little embarrassed. I took a student magazine from the bookshelf and flipped through it casually.

"La la la::::: Fifth grade wins::::: la la la::::: Sixth grade wins:::::"

A loud and noisy sound spread to my eardrums, causing a strong vibration in my heart. I couldn't concentrate on reading anymore.

"I can't restrain myself. Incited by this sound, I also want to join the foolishness," I said to Qin with shame.

"This is everyone's joy. You can't force it," Qin replied kindly.

Walking out of the dormitory, I already saw the surroundings of the playground filled with people. I couldn't see anything inside.

"Xin, why are you coming now? The playground is full of people. Hurry up and come here. You can barely squeeze in one person here. We have already won a goal. Jianmei Bing She.

There is hope for the championship today," Zhen saw me over there, waved to me, and said to me like this.

I squeezed into the crowd. The first thing that caught my eye was the shiny silver championship trophy on the table behind the goal. It was also covered with an exquisite green silk box. Because it was illuminated by the setting sun, it flashed and emitted dazzling light, as if showing off its power. It made so many students abandon their studies to come here to welcome it, support it, and made the players of the two grades sacrifice their energy to be its slaves. Its magic is so great.

"Xin, look how agile Old Wang is. He has already advanced to their territory and is about to score again," Zhen pointed to Old Wang and said to me, interrupting my random thoughts.

"Old Wang's ball skills have improved compared to before."

"Improved a lot."

"Goal!" The surrounding students suddenly shouted like thunder.

"Old Wang is so cute. He scored another one. Let's cheer a few times to boost his morale," Zhen walked up to us and said to a group of people wearing paper hats.

The cheers of the cheerleading squad shifted the attention of the surrounding students. They saw Zhen's inside-out leather robe and the paper hats of the cheerleading squad, and they all opened their mouths and laughed non-stop.

The game started again, and we still had the upper hand. The ball rolled around in their territory. Zhen and the cheerleading squad were shouting and encouraging their courage desperately, shouting until their throats were hoarse, but they still didn't want to stop.

"Shh:::::" Time was up. The referee was blowing his whistle there.

Zhen and the cheerleading squad all ran into the field and picked up Old Wang, sitting him on their shoulders. They were still singing their victory song. Old Wang nodded to his friends with great pride.

The glorious championship trophy had already been taken into the hands of our captain, Xiao Zhuang. In the support and cheers of the students, he walked into the dormitory. The playground, which was once crowded with students, was only left with the lingering sound of shouts and cheers.

Anecdotes from the Zhonggong Uproar Jian Tang

The various newspapers at sea have already reported extensively on the Zhonggong incident. However, there are still one or two trivial matters that seem to need to be recorded by this nameless reporter, so I am now taking up my bare pen and scribbling randomly.

Little Kid to Old Man

When Mr. Yu Youren came to the school to announce his intention to maintain order, he gave a sincere exhortation to more than a thousand students in the sports field (because the auditorium was too small). He said, "...You don't study hard, you just mess around. When you grow a beard as long as mine in the future, you will realize how terrible it is. You are just kids, kids," which attracted the attention of many students. Later, a certain gentleman went to Shanghai and saw two or three representatives of the delegation laughing and talking loudly in the train, seemingly forgetting themselves. So, the gentleman listened respectfully and found them saying,

"He knew about the revolution when he was young. We are doing this, which is also a manifestation of revolution."

"He scolded us for being kids, kids. We can also scold him for being an old man, old man, hahaha..."

The gentleman couldn't help but laugh when he heard this. Later, he told the students, who also made a fuss, and some even wanted to write poetry to praise their genius.

Drooling Three Feet

The day before Mr. Yu Youren arrived at the school, the principal's notice board had two pieces of calligraphy written by Mr. Yu himself, one announcing that he would come to the school to maintain order at a certain time in the afternoon the next day, and one addressed to all the students, both written on Xuan paper and stamped. The students gathered to discuss, some saying,

"Ah, what a beautiful piece of calligraphy! It's a pity I can't get it."

Others said, "Oh, look, it's written on Xuan paper and stamped. This is obviously his way of letting us take it to frame it. However, I don't know if I have the blessing to get it..."

"Yes, do you have that blessing?"

"....Which of us has that kind of blessing?"

"........"

"........"

After such a commotion, the great curtain of night gradually unfolded, and the busy people slowly entered the depths of sleep. At this time, a majestic disciplinary squad, holding a huge wooden stick, ran to the principal's notice board as fast as lightning, hoping to get that precious piece of calligraphy. However, the calligraphy had already "disappeared without a trace." The next morning, many young men and women continued to come to the green glass mirror frame, showing a look of surprise, lingering and reluctant to leave.

Business News

The Huili Company at No. 12 Niuzhuang Road declared that its oil business department has recently invented various kinds of raw materials for daily use, such as raw oil and soybean oil, which are inexpensive and of good quality, and the oil color is smooth and bright. The Shanghai Gramophone Company at No. 15 Zhifu Road declared that it specializes in wholesale distribution of major domestic and foreign brands, with very prosperous sales and a long-standing reputation. It manufactures various artistic gramophones and manages records of famous singers from various companies. The repair department charges low fees and guarantees accuracy. Therefore, the door is crowded with customers every day, and the staff is overwhelmed. All circles who want to buy, please don't miss this opportunity.

The Yuanyuan Hat Shop declared that its Yuanyuan hat made of sea tiger velvet was invented in the 12th year of the Republic of China. The style and manufacturing method have been modified several times before reaching perfection, resulting in considerable losses. It was initially popular among opera fans, and then promoted to literary and art circles. It has been sold in Taicang, Sichuan, Hubei and other places for a long time. Last year, political and business circles in this city also liked to buy and wear it, and business progressed rapidly, with supply falling short of demand, causing many latecomers to regret it. I am sincerely sorry. Now, more products have been added to meet the demand. However, there are shameless people who specialize in imitating and selling goods with imperfect styles and manufacturing methods, filling the market. There have even been cases of counterfeit brands in other cities. Buyers who are unaware are easily deceived. Therefore, we solemnly declare that the Yuanyuan hat has a silk woven yellow background and black letter brand inside. The style is a long cone shape. Those without a brand and with a round surface are counterfeit goods. Please be aware.

Green Garden

The Last Night · Question · Cuckoo

From six to nine in the afternoon is the golden age of our dormitory. Seven or eight classmates surround the stove, reading books or knitting things with yarn. If there were also a pile of peanuts and a few oranges, that would be like possessing the whole world.

Their hands move up and down, with red, green, and various other colors of yarn appearing particularly beautiful under the electric light. The sound of their conversations is as endless as the yarn in their hands. The rest of the people also bury themselves in their books, seemingly oblivious to everything around them. They tilt their heads, appearing very interested, or occasionally jot something down in their notebooks. As for glancing at others, that's just a fleeting moment.

Only S sits quietly in a corner, her face turning red and then white, or suddenly biting her lip and smiling slightly. The meaning expressed by her psychological state is completely unrelated to the environment before her eyes, which is very obvious.

Qian, who sits closest to S, was originally copying something, but often puts down her pen because of her neighbor. She also has a worried look on her face. If the light were not blocked by her book, one could see that her eyes were full of tears.

Hui, who loves to talk the most and is nicknamed "Chatterbox Girl," starts singing:

"Sad is parting, joyful is a new marriage. Silk sister, you are leaving your old friends to establish a new family. Don't you think about how lonely and desolate your Qian will be?"

As her singing stops, the expressions of everyone in the room change. Some stop knitting and say nothing, or gaze at Silk, who is trimming her nails, with a look of affection. Those reading books also put them down, their minds leaving the paradise in the books and returning to the realm of reality.

The atmosphere in the room suddenly becomes tense. Everyone seems to have something to say, but no one can utter a word.

"What's wrong with you all?" Silk asks shyly, her voice as low as a mosquito's hum.

"This is the only night we have to sit together with you. After three years of being classmates, once we separate, not to mention Qian, even we feel very sad." Hen, who is easily moved, suddenly uses her handkerchief to wipe her eyes as she speaks.

"I will come back," Silk says softly. "Yes, studies are important," Hen interjects. Qian buries her head in her book, only her shoulders can be seen shaking slightly.

"Why do people like to get married in winter? Can't they get married at other times?" Chatterbox Girl starts another discussion.

"I don't believe Silk's future 'stool' will also be a person who superstitiously follows old customs. I'm afraid that because he's going to work in the three northeastern provinces, he wants to bring his new wife along to show off even more," this voice comes from behind the stove, it's Huai, the optimist.

"What's so good about it? That fat-headed, big-faced fellow. I get angry when I see him sticking to Silk like a fly to honey. If they don't ask me to see her off next week, fine, but if they ask me to see her off, I'll beat him up to vent my anger," Chatterbox Girl says, actually clenching her fist.

Silk's face turns from white to red, and the scissors in her hand fall, but she doesn't even notice.

"Is she worried or happy? 'A woman's marriage is like being born again.' This is just a proverb, but how can women who don't eat human food and don't know the taste of smoke be an exception? As soon as a woman gets married, her entire life changes. Her behavior and demeanor change, her temperament changes, she simply becomes a different person. Needless to say about old-fashioned marriages, even modern love marriages are no exception. Although I am not a man, let alone a Jia Baoyu-like man, every time I encounter the marriage of my classmates, I always feel extremely heartbroken, and I often sigh secretly, 'Alas, we have lost one more of our kind.' The most precious pink journey of a young girl has come to an end, and even the poetic realm of love will probably disappear from now on. Trivial household chores and the burden of children are all sharp weapons that wear down the flowery youth of women. Not only are they prone to premature aging physically, but even their former bright and vigorous minds will probably be covered with a layer of smoke. Although there are many happy marriages in the world, my prejudice just can't see the joy in them. I always think this is a decaying corpse covered with a brocade canopy: : : :" I was silently thinking about this when something was thrown at my face. Ouch, it's hot, I shouted. I looked and saw that it was a baked sweet potato, so I asked,

"Are there still baked sweet potatoes for sale at this time? It's almost nine o'clock."

"Haha, there are more here. Do you want to buy some?" Huai smiled. It turned out that she had taken some raw sweet potatoes from somewhere and was quietly baking them behind the stove.

"Well-baked, but a bit raw," Chatterbox said.

"You should be happy you even got one to eat," Huai replied.

The depressing atmosphere just now was suddenly broken by the baked sweet potatoes for a while, but it soon returned to its original state. Hen moved her chair closer to Silk, and the two chattered endlessly. Qian's eyes never dried.

The dormitory bell rang, but no one paid attention to it. This is our world. Even if the instructor comes, she can't do anything to us. Anyway, we are not making noise, what are we afraid of her? This shared mentality dominates everyone's actions, so everyone holds on and refuses to say the word "sleep." Usually, by half-past nine, everyone is ostensibly asleep. Tonight, because of the farewell to Silk, everyone feels that the time is too short and wishes they didn't have to sleep. Also, who is willing to be the first to leave this place?

"Tomorrow is Saturday, the workload is light, who cares? Let's sit for a while longer," Huai said, she had finished her task of baking sweet potatoes.

"I won't go to the three northeastern provinces, I will definitely come back before the winter vacation," Silk and Hen's conversation ended with this sentence.

"Hmph, we'll see about that. We don't hope you'll come again, we only ask that when you have new knowledge, you don't forget your old friends altogether, and we'll be grateful for your affection," Hen's voice rose, and her eyes also turned red.

"I'm keeping your bed for you, and I'm preserving the many impressions you gave us. But every time I look at your empty space, how can I not shed tears? You are the sun in our class. After you leave, I feel that the whole world has become dark," the optimistic Huai also complained.

A thin layer of melancholy also covered Silk's joyous face. Her expression seemed like she wanted to cry and also wanted to laugh. In the end, the crying emotion prevailed, and her tears dripped one by one from those beautiful eyes onto her clothes.

The room was quiet, only the cracking sound of the charcoal in the stove broke the silence.

"I'll go tell that stool tomorrow and tell him to roll away himself. Wouldn't it be over if our Silk doesn't get married? You people are all useless, you can't think of a solution," Chatterbox's words made everyone laugh.

Qian and Hen·Silk's tears hung in their eyes, and they also laughed so hard that they leaned back and forth.

"Dang lang, dang lang," the bell outside rang again.

"Why?" I asked.

"Probably because we're not sleeping," Qian finally spoke for the first time this evening, and she was obviously very tired and just wanted to fall on the bed and cry loudly.

Silk stood up as if she had found a savior, picked up the scissors on the ground, and took Qian's arm, preparing to leave first.

"Slow down, this is the last night. Don't be so heartless. Can you just leave without saying goodbye to your many old friends? Hmph, the auspicious day is still early," Chatterbox said indignantly.

"Don't be impatient, the earth will always turn slowly," Huai echoed.

"As long as you say one sentence, I'll let you go. Speak from your heart, is the love of your classmates deeper, or the love of a stool deeper?" Chatterbox said, blocking the door.

"Cla｜｜Classmates' love is deeper," Silk said helplessly in a low voice.

"Haha, let her go," everyone laughed.

Ten o'clock struck, and Silk next door was already asleep. I don't know what she dreamed of, perhaps future happiness.
